./Camera.cxx:void Camera::getHitInfo(HitInfo &hitInfo)
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:{
./Camera.cxx:  float stepSize = 0.1f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  glm::vec3 rayOriginCR = gePositionInWorldCoords();
./Camera.cxx:  glm::vec3 rayDirCR = forwardCR;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  float maxDistanceCR = 5.0f; // Max ray distance
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  for (float t = 0.0f; t < maxDistanceCR; t += stepSize) {
./Camera.cxx:    glm::vec3 point = rayOriginCR + rayDirCR * t;
./Camera.cxx:    BlockCoordinates blockCoords{static_cast<int>(floor(point.x)),
./Camera.cxx:                                 static_cast<int>(floor(point.y)),
./Camera.cxx:                                 static_cast<int>(floor(point.z))};
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:    Voxel *voxel = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal(blockCoords);
./Camera.cxx:    if (voxel && voxel->getBlockType() != AIR) {
./Camera.cxx:      hitInfo.blockCoords = blockCoords;
./Camera.cxx:      hitInfo.hitVoxel = voxel;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:      break;
./Camera.cxx:    }
./Camera.cxx:  }
./Camera.cxx:}

./Camera.cxx:void Camera::updateUBO(UniformBufferObject &UBO, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent,
./Camera.cxx:                       Event &event) {
./Camera.cxx:  static double lastX = event.mouseX;
./Camera.cxx:  static double lastY = event.mouseY;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  float dt = event.dt * 0.001f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  double dx = (lastX - event.mouseX) * !locked;
./Camera.cxx:  double dy = (lastY - event.mouseY) * !locked;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  lastX = event.mouseX;
./Camera.cxx:  lastY = event.mouseY;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  float sensitivity = 0.1f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  yaw += dx * sensitivity;
./Camera.cxx:  if (yaw >= 360)
./Camera.cxx:    yaw -= 360;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  if (yaw < 0)
./Camera.cxx:    yaw += 360;
./Camera.cxx:  // std::cout << "yaw: " << yaw << std::endl;
./Camera.cxx:  pitch += dy * sensitivity;
./Camera.cxx:  pitch = glm::clamp(pitch, -89.9f, 89.9f);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  // Z-up forward vector from yaw/pitch
./Camera.cxx:  forwardCR.x = cos(glm::radians(yaw)) * cos(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:  forwardCR.y = sin(glm::radians(yaw)) * cos(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:  forwardCR.z = sin(glm::radians(pitch));
./Camera.cxx:  forwardCR = glm::normalize(forwardCR);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  glm::vec3 worldUp(0.0f, 0.0f, 1.0f); // Z-up
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  forwardFlat = glm::normalize(glm::vec3(forwardCR.x, forwardCR.y, 0.0f));
./Camera.cxx:  right = glm::normalize(glm::cross(worldUp, forwardFlat));
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  speed = .0054f;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  v_velocity = 30;
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  UBO.view = glm::lookAt(cameraPos, cameraPos + forwardCR, worldUp);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  UBO.proj = glm::perspective(
./Camera.cxx:      glm::radians(90.0f),
./Camera.cxx:      swapChainExtent.width / (float)swapChainExtent.height, 0.025f, 1000.0f);
./Camera.cxx:
./Camera.cxx:  UBO.proj[1][1] *= -1;
./Camera.cxx:}
./Camera.cxx:

./Camera.cxx:  cameraRay.draw(drawInfo);

./Event.cxx:    static auto lastTime = startingTime;
./Event.cxx:
./Event.cxx:    
./Event.cxx:    auto currentTime = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
./Event.cxx:    timeElapsed_ms = std::chrono::duration<double, std::milli>(currentTime - startingTime).count();
./Event.cxx:
./Event.cxx:    auto delta = currentTime - lastTime;
./Event.cxx:    lastTime = currentTime;
./Event.cxx:
./Event.cxx:    dt = std::chrono::duration<double, std::milli>(delta).count();
./Event.cxx:    // std::cout << "Δt = " << dt << std::endl;

./Event.h:class KeyTracker {
./Event.h:    std::unordered_map<int, bool> prevState;
./Event.h:public:
./Event.h:    // Call this once per frame AFTER all key checks
./Event.h:    void update(Event* event, std::initializer_list<int> keys) {
./Event.h:        for (int key : keys)
./Event.h:            prevState[key] = event->getKeyPressed(key);
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:
./Event.h:    bool justPressed(Event* event, int key) {
./Event.h:        return event->getKeyPressed(key) && !prevState[key];
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:
./Event.h:    bool justReleased(Event* event, int key) {
./Event.h:        return !event->getKeyPressed(key) && prevState[key];
./Event.h:    }
./Event.h:};

./GameObjectPool.cxx:Voxel *GameObjectPool::getVoxelGlobal(BlockCoordinates globalCoords)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:{
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    if (globalCoords.z < 0 || globalCoords.z >= 256)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int cox = globalCoords.x >> 4;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int coy = globalCoords.y >> 4;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    Chunk *chunk = terrain->getChunkByKey(Terrain::chunkKey(cox, coy));
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    if (!chunk)
./GameObjectPool.cxx:        return nullptr;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int localX = globalCoords.x & 15;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    int localY = globalCoords.y & 15;
./GameObjectPool.cxx:
./GameObjectPool.cxx:    return &chunk->layers[globalCoords.z].voxels[localX][localY];
./GameObjectPool.cxx:}

./GraphicsPipeline.h:namespace std {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    template<>
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    struct hash<Vertex> {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:        size_t operator()(Vertex const& vertex) const {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            size_t seed = 0;
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            auto hashCombine = [&seed](auto const& v) {
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                seed ^= std::hash<float>()(v)
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + 0x9e3779b97f4a7c15
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed << 6)
./GraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed >> 2);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            };
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.x);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.y);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.z);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.r);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.g);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.b);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.texCoord.x);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.texCoord.y);
./GraphicsPipeline.h:
./GraphicsPipeline.h:            return seed;
./GraphicsPipeline.h:        }
./GraphicsPipeline.h:    };
./GraphicsPipeline.h:}

./Mesh.cxx:void Mesh::createVertexBuffer()
./Mesh.cxx:{
./Mesh.cxx:    stagingVertexBufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (stagingVertexBufferSize == 0)
./Mesh.cxx:        return;
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    // TX
./Mesh.cxx:    utils::createBuffer(stagingVertexBufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_COHERENT_BIT, StagingVertexBuffer, StagingVertexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    // filling in the vertex buffer
./Mesh.cxx:    vkMapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, 0, stagingVertexBufferSize, 0, &stagingVertexBufferData);
./Mesh.cxx:    memcpy(stagingVertexBufferData, vertices.data(), (size_t)stagingVertexBufferSize);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    // creating the actul VBO and setting it up so the it is the destionation of the transfer source
./Mesh.cxx:    // TX
./Mesh.cxx:    utils::createBuffer(stagingVertexBufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_BUFFER_USAGE_VERTEX_BUFFER_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, vertexBuffer, vertexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully
./Mesh.cxx:    utils::copyBuffer(StagingVertexBuffer, vertexBuffer, stagingVertexBufferSize, vkContext);
./Mesh.cxx:}

./Mesh.cxx:        return;

./Mesh.cxx:void Mesh::updateVertexBuffer()
./Mesh.cxx:{
./Mesh.cxx:    VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (bufferSize >= stagingVertexBufferSize)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:        // destroy OLD GPU buffer FIRST
./Mesh.cxx:        if (vertexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:        {
./Mesh.cxx:            vkDeviceWaitIdle(vkContext.device);
./Mesh.cxx:            vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, vertexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:            vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, vertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:            vertexBuffer = VK_NULL_HANDLE;
./Mesh.cxx:            vertexBufferMemory = VK_NULL_HANDLE;
./Mesh.cxx:        }
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:        // now recreate everything
./Mesh.cxx:        createVertexBuffer();
./Mesh.cxx:    }
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (bufferSize == 0)
./Mesh.cxx:        return;
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    memcpy(stagingVertexBufferData, vertices.data(), (size_t)bufferSize);
./Mesh.cxx:    utils::copyBuffer(StagingVertexBuffer, vertexBuffer, bufferSize, vkContext);
./Mesh.cxx:}
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:void Mesh::updateIndexBuffer()
./Mesh.cxx:{
./Mesh.cxx:    VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(indices[0]) * indices.size();
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (bufferSize >= stagingIndexBufferSize)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:        if (indexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:        {
./Mesh.cxx:            vkDeviceWaitIdle(vkContext.device);
./Mesh.cxx:            vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, indexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:            vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, indexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:            indexBuffer = VK_NULL_HANDLE;
./Mesh.cxx:            indexBufferMemory = VK_NULL_HANDLE;
./Mesh.cxx:        }
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:        createIndexBuffer();
./Mesh.cxx:    }
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (bufferSize == 0)
./Mesh.cxx:        return;
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    memcpy(stagingIndexBufferData, indices.data(), (size_t)bufferSize);
./Mesh.cxx:    utils::copyBuffer(StagingIndexBuffer, indexBuffer, bufferSize, vkContext);
./Mesh.cxx:}

./Mesh.cxx:void Mesh::draw(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer, VkPipelineLayout pipelineLayout, VkPipeline graphicsPipeline, std::vector<VkDescriptorSet> &descriptorSets, uint32_t currentFrame, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, PushConstantC1 &c1)
./Mesh.cxx:{
./Mesh.cxx:    VkBuffer vertexBuffers[] = {vertexBuffer};
./Mesh.cxx:    VkDeviceSize offsets[] = {0};
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    [[unlikely]] if (vertices.size() == 0 || indices.size() == 0)
./Mesh.cxx:        return;
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    vkCmdBindVertexBuffers(commandBuffer, 0, 1, vertexBuffers, offsets);
./Mesh.cxx:    vkCmdBindIndexBuffer(commandBuffer, indexBuffer, 0, VK_INDEX_TYPE_UINT32);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    vkCmdPushConstants(commandBuffer, pipelineLayout, VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT, 0, sizeof(PushConstantC1), &c1);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    vkCmdBindDescriptorSets(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, pipelineLayout,
./Mesh.cxx:                            0, 1, &(descriptorSets[currentFrame]), 0, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    vkCmdDrawIndexed(commandBuffer, static_cast<uint32_t>(indices.size()), 1, 0, 0, 0);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:}

./Mesh.cxx:void Mesh::cleanup()
./Mesh.cxx:{
./Mesh.cxx:    if (StagingVertexBufferMemory != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:        vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory);
./Mesh.cxx:    if (StagingIndexBufferMemory != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:        vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory);
./Mesh.cxx:
./Mesh.cxx:    if (indexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, indexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, indexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:    }
./Mesh.cxx:    if (vertexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, vertexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, vertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:    }
./Mesh.cxx:    if (StagingIndexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:    }
./Mesh.cxx:    if (StagingVertexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./Mesh.cxx:    {
./Mesh.cxx:        vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBuffer, nullptr);
./Mesh.cxx:        vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, nullptr);

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:void RayGraphicsPipeline::createGraphicsPipeline()
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    std::cout << "Creating Ray Graphics Pipeline..." << std::endl;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    auto vertShaderCode = readFile("/home/divyansh/MinecraftClone/shaders/simple_shader_ray_v.spv");
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    auto fragShaderCode = readFile("/home/divyansh/MinecraftClone/shaders/simple_shader_ray_f.spv");
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkShaderModule vertShaderModule = createShaderModule(vertShaderCode);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkShaderModule fragShaderModule = createShaderModule(fragShaderCode);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // shaderStageCreation
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo vertShaderStageInfo{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_SHADER_STAGE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.stage = VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT; // telling vulkan 'which stage must this shader go'
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.module = vertShaderModule;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertShaderStageInfo.pName = "main";
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo fragShaderStageInfo{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_SHADER_STAGE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.stage = VK_SHADER_STAGE_FRAGMENT_BIT;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.module = fragShaderModule;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    fragShaderStageInfo.pName = "main";
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineShaderStageCreateInfo shaderStages[] = {vertShaderStageInfo, fragShaderStageInfo};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    auto bindingDescription = RayPoints::getBindingDescription();
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    auto attributeDescriptions = RayPoints::getAttributeDescriptions();
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineVertexInputStateCreateInfo vertexInputInfo{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertexInputInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_VERTEX_INPUT_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertexInputInfo.vertexBindingDescriptionCount = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertexInputInfo.vertexAttributeDescriptionCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(attributeDescriptions.size());
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertexInputInfo.pVertexBindingDescriptions = &bindingDescription;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vertexInputInfo.pVertexAttributeDescriptions = attributeDescriptions.data();
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // input assembly
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineInputAssemblyStateCreateInfo inputAssembly{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    inputAssembly.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_INPUT_ASSEMBLY_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    inputAssembly.topology = VK_PRIMITIVE_TOPOLOGY_LINE_LIST;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    inputAssembly.primitiveRestartEnable = VK_FALSE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // viewport and scissors
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkViewport viewport{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.x = .0f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.y = .0f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.width = (float)swapChainExtent.width;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.height = (float)swapChainExtent.height; // this swapchain is used as a framebuffer hensforth using it as the size for our viewport
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.minDepth = .0f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewport.maxDepth = 1.0f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkRect2D scissor{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    scissor.offset = {0, 0};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    scissor.extent = swapChainExtent;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // //dyanmic scissor and viewport
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // std::vector<VkDynamicState> dynamicStates =
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //     VK_DYNAMIC_STATE_VIEWPORT,
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //     VK_DYNAMIC_STATE_SCISSOR
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // };
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // VkPipelineDynamicStateCreateInfo dynamicState{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // dynamicState.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_DYNAMIC_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // dynamicState.dynamicStateCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(dynamicStates.size());
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // dynamicState.pDynamicStates = dynamicStates.data();
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineViewportStateCreateInfo viewportState{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewportState.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_VIEWPORT_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewportState.viewportCount = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewportState.pViewports = &viewport;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewportState.scissorCount = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    viewportState.pScissors = &scissor;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // Rasterizer
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineRasterizationStateCreateInfo rasterizer{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_RASTERIZATION_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.depthClampEnable = VK_FALSE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.rasterizerDiscardEnable = VK_FALSE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.polygonMode = VK_POLYGON_MODE_FILL;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.lineWidth = 1.0f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.cullMode = VK_CULL_MODE_BACK_BIT;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.frontFace = VK_FRONT_FACE_COUNTER_CLOCKWISE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    rasterizer.depthBiasEnable = VK_FALSE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // MSSA(disabled for now)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineMultisampleStateCreateInfo multisampling{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    multisampling.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_MULTISAMPLE_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    multisampling.sampleShadingEnable = VK_FALSE;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    multisampling.rasterizationSamples = msaaSamples;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    multisampling.minSampleShading = .2f;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineDepthStencilStateCreateInfo depthStencil{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    depthStencil.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_DEPTH_STENCIL_STATE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    depthStencil.depthTestEnable = VK_TRUE;

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    colorBlendAttachment.colorWriteMask = VK_COLOR_COMPONENT_R_BIT | VK_COLOR_COMPONENT_G_BIT | VK_COLOR_COMPONENT_B_BIT | VK_COLOR_COMPONENT_A_BIT;

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // Pipeline Layout
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    //(passing data to uniform objects in shaders)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPipelineLayoutCreateInfo pipelineLayoutInfo{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineLayoutInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PIPELINE_LAYOUT_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineLayoutInfo.setLayoutCount = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineLayoutInfo.pSetLayouts = descriptorSetLayout;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkPushConstantRange pushConstatn;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pushConstatn.offset = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pushConstatn.size = sizeof(PushConstantC1);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pushConstatn.stageFlags = VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineLayoutInfo.pPushConstantRanges = &pushConstatn;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineLayoutInfo.pushConstantRangeCount = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    if (vkCreatePipelineLayout(device, &pipelineLayoutInfo, nullptr, &pipelineLayout) != VK_SUCCESS)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create pipeline layout!");
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    }
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // creating graphics pipeline
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkGraphicsPipelineCreateInfo pipelineInfo{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_GRAPHICS_PIPELINE_CREATE_INFO;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.stageCount = 2; // the shader stage count
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pStages = shaderStages;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pVertexInputState = &vertexInputInfo;

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pViewportState = &viewportState;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pRasterizationState = &rasterizer;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pMultisampleState = &multisampling;

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.pColorBlendState = &colorBlending;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // pipelineInfo.pDynamicState = &dynamic_state;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.layout = pipelineLayout;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.renderPass = renderPass; // passs the render pass
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    pipelineInfo.subpass = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    if (vkCreateGraphicsPipelines(device, VK_NULL_HANDLE, 1, &pipelineInfo, nullptr, &graphicsPipeline) != VK_SUCCESS)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create graphics pipeline!");
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    }
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vkDestroyShaderModule(device, fragShaderModule, nullptr);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    vkDestroyShaderModule(device, vertShaderModule, nullptr);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:}

./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription RayPoints::getBindingDescription()
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(RayPoints);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:}
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 2> RayPoints::getAttributeDescriptions()
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    std::array<VkVertexInputAttributeDescription, 2> attributeDescriptions{};
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].binding = 0;                         // same as getBindingDescription
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].location = 0;                        // directly co-relates to 'layout(location = 0)'
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[0].offset = offsetof(RayPoints, pos);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].binding = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].location = 1;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].format = VK_FORMAT_R32G32B32_SFLOAT; // vec3
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    attributeDescriptions[1].offset = offsetof(RayPoints, color);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return attributeDescriptions;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.cxx:}

./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:namespace std {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:    template<>
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:    struct hash<RayPoints> {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:        size_t operator()(RayPoints const& vertex) const {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            size_t seed = 0;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            auto hashCombine = [&seed](auto const& v) {
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:                seed ^= std::hash<float>()(v)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:                      + 0x9e3779b97f4a7c15
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed << 6)
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:                      + (seed >> 2);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            };
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.x);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.y);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.z);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.r);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.g);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.color.b);
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:            return seed;
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:        }
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:    };
./RayGraphicsPipeline.h:}

./RayMesher.cxx:void RayMesher::createVertexBuffer()
./RayMesher.cxx:{
./RayMesher.cxx:    VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    if (bufferSize == 0)
./RayMesher.cxx:        return;
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    // TX
./RayMesher.cxx:    utils::createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_CACHED_BIT, StagingVertexBuffer, StagingVertexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    // filling in the vertex buffer
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkMapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, 0, bufferSize, 0, &stagingVertexBufferData);
./RayMesher.cxx:    memcpy(stagingVertexBufferData, vertices.data(), (size_t)bufferSize);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    // creating the actul VBO and setting it up so the it is the destionation of the transfer source
./RayMesher.cxx:    // TX
./RayMesher.cxx:    utils::createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_BUFFER_USAGE_VERTEX_BUFFER_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, vertexBuffer, vertexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully
./RayMesher.cxx:    utils::copyBuffer(StagingVertexBuffer, vertexBuffer, bufferSize, vkContext);
./RayMesher.cxx:}
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:void RayMesher::createIndexBuffer()
./RayMesher.cxx:{
./RayMesher.cxx:    VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(indices[0]) * indices.size();

./RayMesher.cxx:    if (bufferSize == 0)
./RayMesher.cxx:        return;
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    utils::createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT, VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT | VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_CACHED_BIT, StagingIndexBuffer, StagingIndexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:

./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:void RayMesher::draw(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer, VkPipelineLayout pipelineLayout, VkPipeline graphicsPipeline, std::vector<VkDescriptorSet> &descriptorSets, uint32_t currentFrame, VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, PushConstantC1 &c1)
./RayMesher.cxx:{
./RayMesher.cxx:    VkBuffer vertexBuffers[] = {vertexBuffer};
./RayMesher.cxx:    VkDeviceSize offsets[] = {0};
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    [[unlikely]] if (vertices.size() == 0 || indices.size() == 0)
./RayMesher.cxx:        return;
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdBindVertexBuffers(commandBuffer, 0, 1, vertexBuffers, offsets);
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdBindIndexBuffer(commandBuffer, indexBuffer, 0, VK_INDEX_TYPE_UINT32);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdPushConstants(commandBuffer, pipelineLayout, VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT, 0, sizeof(PushConstantC1), &c1);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdBindDescriptorSets(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, pipelineLayout,
./RayMesher.cxx:                            0, 1, &(descriptorSets[currentFrame]), 0, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkCmdDrawIndexed(commandBuffer, static_cast<uint32_t>(indices.size()), 1, 0, 0, 0);
./RayMesher.cxx:}

./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, vertexBuffer, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, vertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBuffer, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBuffer, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./RayMesher.cxx:}

./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::generateChunks() {
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  int nChunks = 0;
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  for (int x = -RENDER_DISTANCE; x <= RENDER_DISTANCE; x++) {
./Terrain.cxx:    for (int y = -RENDER_DISTANCE; y <= RENDER_DISTANCE; y++) {
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:      Chunk *c = new Chunk(x, y, vkContext, gop);
./Terrain.cxx:      chunks.emplace(chunkKey(x, y), c);
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:      c->makeVisible();
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:      c->generateMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:      c->createBuffers();
./Terrain.cxx:      nChunks++;
./Terrain.cxx:    }
./Terrain.cxx:  }
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  // Chunk *c = new Chunk(0, 0, vkContext, gop);
./Terrain.cxx:  // chunks.emplace(chunkKey(0, 0), c);
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  // c->makeVisible();
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  // c->generateMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:  // c->createBuffers();
./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  ready = true;
./Terrain.cxx:  fmt::println("total chunks created is: {}", nChunks);
./Terrain.cxx:}

./Terrain.cxx:void Terrain::updateChunkMesh(int cmx, int cmy) {
./Terrain.cxx:  auto it = chunks.find(chunkKey(cmx, cmy));
./Terrain.cxx:  if (it == chunks.end())
./Terrain.cxx:    return;
./Terrain.cxx:

./Terrain.cxx:
./Terrain.cxx:  chunk->updateChunkMesh();
./Terrain.cxx:}

./UIComponents.cxx:void UIComponents::createVertexBuffer() {
./UIComponents.cxx:  stagingVertexBufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (stagingVertexBufferSize == 0)
./UIComponents.cxx:    return;
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  // TX
./UIComponents.cxx:  utils::createBuffer(stagingVertexBufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT |
./UIComponents.cxx:                          VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_COHERENT_BIT,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      StagingVertexBuffer, StagingVertexBufferMemory,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      vkContext);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  // filling in the vertex buffer
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkMapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, 0,
./UIComponents.cxx:              stagingVertexBufferSize, 0, &stagingVertexBufferData);
./UIComponents.cxx:  memcpy(stagingVertexBufferData, vertices.data(),
./UIComponents.cxx:         (size_t)stagingVertexBufferSize);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  // creating the actul VBO and setting it up so the it is the destionation of
./UIComponents.cxx:  // the transfer source TX
./UIComponents.cxx:  utils::createBuffer(stagingVertexBufferSize,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT |
./UIComponents.cxx:                          VK_BUFFER_USAGE_VERTEX_BUFFER_BIT,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, vertexBuffer,
./UIComponents.cxx:                      vertexBufferMemory, vkContext);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully
./UIComponents.cxx:  utils::copyBuffer(StagingVertexBuffer, vertexBuffer, stagingVertexBufferSize,
./UIComponents.cxx:                    vkContext);
./UIComponents.cxx:}

./UIComponents.cxx:void UIComponents::initUIComponent(glm::vec2 position, glm::vec2 size) {
./UIComponents.cxx:  vertices.clear();
./UIComponents.cxx:  indices.clear();
./UIComponents.cxx:  vertices.reserve(4);
./UIComponents.cxx:  indices.reserve(6);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  this->position = position;
./UIComponents.cxx:  this->size = size;
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  float cx = position.x - size.x / 2;
./UIComponents.cxx:  float cy = position.y - size.y / 2;
./UIComponents.cxx:  float w = size.x, h = size.y;
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  float z = -.1f + espilon_dz;
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  vertices = {
./UIComponents.cxx:      {{cx, cy, z}, {0.0f, 0.0f}, (uint32_t)textureIDX},         // bottom-left
./UIComponents.cxx:      {{cx, cy + h, z}, {0.0f, 1.0f}, (uint32_t)textureIDX},     // top-left
./UIComponents.cxx:      {{cx + w, cy + h, z}, {1.0f, 1.0f}, (uint32_t)textureIDX}, // top-right
./UIComponents.cxx:      {{cx + w, cy, z}, {1.0f, 0.0f}, (uint32_t)textureIDX},     // bottom-right
./UIComponents.cxx:  };
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  indices = {0, 1, 2, 2, 3, 0};
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  createVertexBuffer();
./UIComponents.cxx:  createIndexBuffer();
./UIComponents.cxx:}

./UIComponents.cxx:void UIComponents::draw(DrawInfo &drawInfo,
./UIComponents.cxx:                        PushConstantC2 &c2) {
./UIComponents.cxx:  VkBuffer vertexBuffers[] = {vertexBuffer};
./UIComponents.cxx:  VkDeviceSize offsets[] = {0};
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (vertices.size() == 0 || indices.size() == 0) [[unlikely]]
./UIComponents.cxx:    return;
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkCmdBindVertexBuffers(drawInfo.commandBuffer, 0, 1, vertexBuffers, offsets);
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkCmdBindIndexBuffer(drawInfo.commandBuffer, indexBuffer, 0, VK_INDEX_TYPE_UINT32);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkCmdPushConstants(drawInfo.commandBuffer, drawInfo.pipelineLayout, VK_SHADER_STAGE_VERTEX_BIT,
./UIComponents.cxx:                     0, sizeof(PushConstantC2), &c2);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkCmdBindDescriptorSets(drawInfo.commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS,
./UIComponents.cxx:                          drawInfo.pipelineLayout, 0, 1, &(drawInfo.descriptorSets[drawInfo.currentFrame]),
./UIComponents.cxx:                          0, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  vkCmdDrawIndexed(drawInfo.commandBuffer, static_cast<uint32_t>(indices.size()),
./UIComponents.cxx:                   instanceCount, 0, 0, 0);
./UIComponents.cxx:}

./UIComponents.cxx:void UIComponents::cleanup() {
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (StagingVertexBufferMemory != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory);
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (StagingIndexBufferMemory != VK_NULL_HANDLE)
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory);
./UIComponents.cxx:
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (indexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE) {
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, indexBuffer, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, indexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:  }
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (vertexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE) {
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, vertexBuffer, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, vertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:  }
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (StagingIndexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE) {
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBuffer, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingIndexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:  }
./UIComponents.cxx:  if (StagingVertexBuffer != VK_NULL_HANDLE) {
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkDestroyBuffer(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBuffer, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:    vkFreeMemory(vkContext.device, StagingVertexBufferMemory, nullptr);
./UIComponents.cxx:  }

./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription UIVertex::getBindingDescription()
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:{
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(UIVertex);
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./UIRenderPipeline.cxx:}

./UIRenderPipeline.h:        size_t operator()(UIVertex const& vertex) const {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            size_t seed = 0;
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            auto hashCombine = [&seed](auto const& v) {
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                seed ^= std::hash<float>()(v)
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + 0x9e3779b97f4a7c15
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + (seed << 6)
./UIRenderPipeline.h:                      + (seed >> 2);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            };
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.x);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.y);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.pos.z);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.uv.r);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:            hashCombine(vertex.uv.g);
./UIRenderPipeline.h:

./UIRenderPipeline.h:        }

./intiVK2.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};

./intiVK2.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;

./intiVK2.cxx:    vkQueueSubmit(graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE);
./intiVK2.cxx:    vkQueueWaitIdle(graphicsQueue);

./intiVK2.cxx:    vkFreeCommandBuffers(device, commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);

./intiVk3.cxx:// In a swapchain we only use color images as that is all the is need to simply
./intiVk3.cxx:// draw on the screen Depth buffers and other stuff is handled in other places
./intiVk3.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createSwapChain() {
./intiVk3.cxx:  std::cout << "Creating Swap Chain..." << std::endl;
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- get the swapchain capabilities
./intiVk3.cxx:  SwapChainSupportDetails swapChainSupport =
./intiVk3.cxx:      querySwapChainSupport(physicalDevice);
./intiVk3.cxx:  // pick the best options
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkSurfaceFormatKHR surfaceFormat =
./intiVk3.cxx:      chooseSwapSurfaceFormat(swapChainSupport.formats);
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkPresentModeKHR presentMode =
./intiVk3.cxx:      chooseSwapPresentMode(swapChainSupport.presentModes);
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkExtent2D extent = chooseSwapExtent(swapChainSupport.capabilities);
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- save the format and extent ----
./intiVk3.cxx:  swapChainImageFormat = surfaceFormat.format;
./intiVk3.cxx:  swapChainExtent = extent;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // add one to allow triple buffering
./intiVk3.cxx:  // Metal limits the max to 3 so only +1 one is allowed while NVIDIA and AMD
./intiVk3.cxx:  // has no limits
./intiVk3.cxx:  uint32_t imageCount = swapChainSupport.capabilities.minImageCount + 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // Check to not exeed the maximum
./intiVk3.cxx:  // 0 is a special number meaning that there is not upper limit
./intiVk3.cxx:  if (swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount > 0 &&
./intiVk3.cxx:      imageCount > swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount) {
./intiVk3.cxx:    imageCount = swapChainSupport.capabilities.maxImageCount;
./intiVk3.cxx:  }
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkSwapchainCreateInfoKHR createInfo{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SWAPCHAIN_CREATE_INFO_KHR;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.surface = surface; // surface
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- Image settings ----
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.minImageCount = imageCount;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.imageFormat = surfaceFormat.format;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.imageColorSpace = surfaceFormat.colorSpace;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.imageExtent = extent;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.imageArrayLayers = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.imageUsage =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_IMAGE_USAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_BIT; // for post VFX use
./intiVk3.cxx:                                           // VK_IMAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- graphics and present queue familiy equality check
./intiVk3.cxx:  QueueFamilyIndices indices = findQueueFamilies(physicalDevice);
./intiVk3.cxx:  uint32_t queueFamilyIndices[] = {indices.graphicsFamily.value(),
./intiVk3.cxx:                                   indices.presentFamily.value()};
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // If not same then use concurrent which means that we dont have to worry
./intiVk3.cxx:  // about the manual ownership If same then use exclusive which is faster
./intiVk3.cxx:  if (indices.graphicsFamily != indices.presentFamily) {
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.imageSharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_CONCURRENT;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.queueFamilyIndexCount = 2;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.pQueueFamilyIndices = queueFamilyIndices;
./intiVk3.cxx:  } else {
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.imageSharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.queueFamilyIndexCount = 0;     // Optional
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.pQueueFamilyIndices = nullptr; // Optional
./intiVk3.cxx:  }
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // how to transform the present
./intiVk3.cxx:  // IE: tell vulkan how to handle rotations. We just use what the windowing
./intiVk3.cxx:  // system provides
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.preTransform = swapChainSupport.capabilities.currentTransform;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.compositeAlpha =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_COMPOSITE_ALPHA_OPAQUE_BIT_KHR; // how shall this window blend with
./intiVk3.cxx:                                         // other windows
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.presentMode = presentMode;
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.clipped =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_TRUE; // don't care about the pixels that are not seen on the screen
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  createInfo.oldSwapchain = VK_NULL_HANDLE; // later stuff
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  if (vkCreateSwapchainKHR(device, &createInfo, nullptr, &swapChain) !=
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_SUCCESS) {
./intiVk3.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to create swap chain!");
./intiVk3.cxx:  }
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- Retrive the images ----
./intiVk3.cxx:  vkGetSwapchainImagesKHR(device, swapChain, &imageCount, nullptr);
./intiVk3.cxx:  swapChainImages.resize(imageCount);
./intiVk3.cxx:  vkGetSwapchainImagesKHR(device, swapChain, &imageCount,
./intiVk3.cxx:                          swapChainImages.data());
./intiVk3.cxx:}
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:// Images views: VkImage is just raw memory. Image views provide the GPU with
./intiVk3.cxx:// all the neseccary context and information to present the data correctly We
./intiVk3.cxx:// did specify in the swapchain what formats and options to use, then why an
./intiVk3.cxx:// image view? Because a VkImage by itself proved no indication of the location
./intiVk3.cxx:// and size of the contents An Image view providies those important information
./intiVk3.cxx:// to the GPU
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createImageViews() {
./intiVk3.cxx:  std::cout << "Creating Image Views..." << std::endl;
./intiVk3.cxx:  swapChainImageViews.resize(swapChainImages.size());
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  for (size_t i = 0; i < swapChainImages.size(); i++) {
./intiVk3.cxx:    VkImageViewCreateInfo createInfo{};
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_VIEW_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.image = swapChainImages[i];
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:    // specifing how shall the images be interpreted
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.viewType = VK_IMAGE_VIEW_TYPE_2D;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:    // mapping the color channels to defaults
./intiVk3.cxx:    // VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY → use the original channel layout.
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.components.r = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.components.g = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.components.b = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.components.a = VK_COMPONENT_SWIZZLE_IDENTITY;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:    // specifing how shall the images be use(their purpose)
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.subresourceRange.aspectMask =
./intiVk3.cxx:        VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT; // color targets
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = 0;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./intiVk3.cxx:    createInfo.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:    if (vkCreateImageView(device, &createInfo, nullptr,
./intiVk3.cxx:                          &swapChainImageViews[i]) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./intiVk3.cxx:      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to create image views");
./intiVk3.cxx:    }
./intiVk3.cxx:  }
./intiVk3.cxx:}

./intiVk3.cxx:// Render pass
./intiVk3.cxx:// It tells vulkan what attachment to use
./intiVk3.cxx:// How to use
./intiVk3.cxx:// Layout transitions
./intiVk3.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createRenderPass() {
./intiVk3.cxx:  std::cout << "Creating Render Pass..." << std::endl;
./intiVk3.cxx:  // ---- describing what rescources we will be using ----
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentDescription depthAttachment{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.format = VK_FORMAT_D32_SFLOAT;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.samples = msaaSamples;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.loadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_CLEAR;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.storeOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachment.finalLayout =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentReference depthAttachmentRef{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachmentRef.attachment = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:  depthAttachmentRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentDescription colorAttachment{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.samples = msaaSamples;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.loadOp =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_CLEAR; // what to do with the framebuffer after the
./intiVk3.cxx:                                   // render pass has started
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.storeOp =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_STORE; // what to do with the memory(store it in
./intiVk3.cxx:                                    // the vram or not)
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  // don't care about the stencil
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachment.finalLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentReference colorAttachmentRef{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentRef.attachment = 0; // IDX to the attachment
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentDescription colorAttachmentResolve{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.format = swapChainImageFormat;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.samples = VK_SAMPLE_COUNT_1_BIT;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.loadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.storeOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_STORE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.stencilLoadOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_LOAD_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.stencilStoreOp = VK_ATTACHMENT_STORE_OP_DONT_CARE;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.initialLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolve.finalLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_PRESENT_SRC_KHR;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkAttachmentReference colorAttachmentResolveRef{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolveRef.attachment = 2;
./intiVk3.cxx:  colorAttachmentResolveRef.layout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OPTIMAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkSubpassDescription subpass{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  subpass.pipelineBindPoint =
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS; // alternative is compute
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  subpass.colorAttachmentCount = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:  subpass.pColorAttachments = &colorAttachmentRef;
./intiVk3.cxx:  subpass.pDepthStencilAttachment = &depthAttachmentRef;
./intiVk3.cxx:  subpass.pResolveAttachments = &colorAttachmentResolveRef;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  std::array<VkAttachmentDescription, 3> attachments = {
./intiVk3.cxx:      colorAttachment, depthAttachment, colorAttachmentResolve};
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkRenderPassCreateInfo renderPassInfo{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_RENDER_PASS_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.attachmentCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(attachments.size());
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.pAttachments = attachments.data();
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.subpassCount = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.pSubpasses = &subpass;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  VkSubpassDependency dependency{};
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.srcSubpass = VK_SUBPASS_EXTERNAL;
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.dstSubpass = 0;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.srcStageMask = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OUTPUT_BIT |
./intiVk3.cxx:                            VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_LATE_FRAGMENT_TESTS_BIT;
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_WRITE_BIT |
./intiVk3.cxx:                             VK_ACCESS_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_WRITE_BIT;
./intiVk3.cxx:  ;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.dstStageMask = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OUTPUT_BIT |
./intiVk3.cxx:                            VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_EARLY_FRAGMENT_TESTS_BIT;
./intiVk3.cxx:  dependency.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_WRITE_BIT |
./intiVk3.cxx:                             VK_ACCESS_DEPTH_STENCIL_ATTACHMENT_WRITE_BIT;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.dependencyCount = 1;
./intiVk3.cxx:  renderPassInfo.pDependencies = &dependency;
./intiVk3.cxx:
./intiVk3.cxx:  if (vkCreateRenderPass(device, &renderPassInfo, nullptr, &renderPass) !=
./intiVk3.cxx:      VK_SUCCESS) {
./intiVk3.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to create render pass!");
./intiVk3.cxx:  }
./intiVk3.cxx:}

./utils.cxx:void utils::createBuffer(VkDeviceSize size, VkBufferUsageFlags usage, VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties, VkBuffer &buffer, VkDeviceMemory &bufferMemory, VulkanContext &vkContext)
./utils.cxx:{
./utils.cxx:    VkBufferCreateInfo bufferInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_BUFFER_CREATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.size = size;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.usage = usage;
./utils.cxx:    bufferInfo.sharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkCreateBuffer(vkContext.device, &bufferInfo, nullptr, &buffer) != VK_SUCCESS)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to create buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkMemoryRequirements memRequirements;
./utils.cxx:    vkGetBufferMemoryRequirements(vkContext.device, buffer, &memRequirements);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkMemoryAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_MEMORY_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.allocationSize = memRequirements.size;
./utils.cxx:    uint32_t typeFilter = memRequirements.memoryTypeBits;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./utils.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(vkContext.physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags & properties) == properties)
./utils.cxx:        {
./utils.cxx:            allocInfo.memoryTypeIndex = i;
./utils.cxx:            goto _ok;
./utils.cxx:        }
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./utils.cxx:    _ok:;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkAllocateMemory(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, nullptr, &bufferMemory) != VK_SUCCESS)
./utils.cxx:    {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate buffer memory!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    vkBindBufferMemory(vkContext.device, buffer, bufferMemory, 0);
./utils.cxx:}
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:void utils::copyBuffer(VkBuffer srcBuffer, VkBuffer dstBuffer, VkDeviceSize size, VulkanContext &vkContext)
./utils.cxx:{
./utils.cxx:    // 1. Create a temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.commandPool = vkContext.commandPool; // your command pool
./utils.cxx:    allocInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:    if (vkAllocateCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, &commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 2. Begin the command buffer
./utils.cxx:    VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    beginInfo.flags = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_USAGE_ONE_TIME_SUBMIT_BIT;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkBeginCommandBuffer(commandBuffer, &beginInfo) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to begin command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 3. Define the copy region
./utils.cxx:    VkBufferCopy copyRegion{};
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.srcOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.dstOffset = 0; // optional
./utils.cxx:    copyRegion.size = size;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 4. Record the copy command
./utils.cxx:    vkCmdCopyBuffer(commandBuffer, srcBuffer, dstBuffer, 1, &copyRegion);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 5. End the command buffer
./utils.cxx:    if (vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to end command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 6. Submit the command buffer and wait
./utils.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./utils.cxx:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffer;
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    if (vkQueueSubmit(vkContext.graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./utils.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit copy command buffer!");
./utils.cxx:    }
./utils.cxx:    vkQueueWaitIdle(vkContext.graphicsQueue);
./utils.cxx:
./utils.cxx:    // 7. Free the temporary command buffer
./utils.cxx:    vkFreeCommandBuffers(vkContext.device, vkContext.commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);
./utils.cxx:}

./Player.cxx:void Player::handlePlayerMovement(UniformBufferObject &UBO,
./Player.cxx:                                  VkExtent2D &swapChainExtent, Event &event) {
./Player.cxx:  static float deltaJZ = 0;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  double dx = 0, dy = 0, dz = 0;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  selfTransform.position = camera->cameraPos;
./Player.cxx:  selfTransform.position.z += .2f;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  aabb.max = selfTransform.position + glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, .0f);
./Player.cxx:  aabb.min = selfTransform.position - glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  AxisAlignedBoundingBox groundAABB{};
./Player.cxx:  groundAABB.max = selfTransform.position + glm::vec3(.1f, .1f, .0f);
./Player.cxx:  groundAABB.min = selfTransform.position - glm::vec3(.1f, .1f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  // ── ground check ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:  playerState.onGround = false;
./Player.cxx:  {
./Player.cxx:    int feet = floor(groundAABB.min.z);
./Player.cxx:    int head = floor(groundAABB.max.z);
./Player.cxx:    int minX = floor(groundAABB.min.x);
./Player.cxx:    int maxX = floor(groundAABB.max.x);
./Player.cxx:    int minY = floor(groundAABB.min.y);
./Player.cxx:    int maxY = floor(groundAABB.max.y);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    for (int k = feet; k <= head && !playerState.onGround; k++)
./Player.cxx:      for (int i = minX; i <= maxX && !playerState.onGround; i++)
./Player.cxx:        for (int j = minY; j <= maxY; j++) {
./Player.cxx:          auto v = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({i, j, k});
./Player.cxx:          if (v && v->blockType != AIR) {
./Player.cxx:            playerState.onGround = true;
./Player.cxx:            break;
./Player.cxx:          }
./Player.cxx:        }
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  // ── gravity / jump ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:  if (!playerState.onGround && !playerState.inJump)
./Player.cxx:    dz -= .01f * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:  else if (playerState.inJump) {
./Player.cxx:    deltaJZ -= .003f * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:    dz += .01f * event.dt * deltaJZ;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  // ── desired XY movement ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:  float x_fac = cos(glm::radians(camera->yaw));
./Player.cxx:  float y_fac = sin(glm::radians(camera->yaw));
./Player.cxx:  float x_fac_dx = x_fac * camera->speed * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:  float y_fac_dy = y_fac * camera->speed * event.dt;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  // Update facing direction for animation / other systems — NOT used for
./Player.cxx:  // collision
./Player.cxx:  bool xDominant = std::abs(x_fac) > std::abs(y_fac);
./Player.cxx:  if (x_fac > 0 && xDominant)
./Player.cxx:    facingDirection = NORTH;
./Player.cxx:  else if (x_fac < 0 && xDominant)
./Player.cxx:    facingDirection = SOUTH;
./Player.cxx:  else if (y_fac > 0 && !xDominant)
./Player.cxx:    facingDirection = WEST;
./Player.cxx:  else if (y_fac < 0 && !xDominant)
./Player.cxx:    facingDirection = EAST;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  bool KEY_W = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_W);
./Player.cxx:  bool KEY_S = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_S);
./Player.cxx:  bool KEY_A = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_A);
./Player.cxx:  bool KEY_D = event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_D);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (KEY_W) {
./Player.cxx:    dx += x_fac_dx;
./Player.cxx:    dy += y_fac_dy;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:  if (KEY_S) {
./Player.cxx:    dx -= x_fac_dx;
./Player.cxx:    dy -= y_fac_dy;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:  if (KEY_A) {
./Player.cxx:    dx += -y_fac_dy;
./Player.cxx:    dy += x_fac_dx;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:  if (KEY_D) {
./Player.cxx:    dx -= -y_fac_dy;
./Player.cxx:    dy -= x_fac_dx;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  // ── axis-separated collision ─────────────────────────────────────────────
./Player.cxx:  // Helper: does the AABB at `testPos` overlap any solid voxel?
./Player.cxx:  auto overlaps = [&](glm::vec3 testPos) -> bool {
./Player.cxx:    glm::vec3 tMax = testPos + glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, .0f);
./Player.cxx:    glm::vec3 tMin = testPos - glm::vec3(.25f, .25f, 1.8f);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    int x0 = floor(tMin.x), x1 = floor(tMax.x);
./Player.cxx:    int y0 = floor(tMin.y), y1 = floor(tMax.y);
./Player.cxx:    int z0 = floor(tMin.z) + 1, z1 = floor(tMax.z);
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:    for (int k = z0; k <= z1; k++)
./Player.cxx:      for (int i = x0; i <= x1; i++)
./Player.cxx:        for (int j = y0; j <= y1; j++) {
./Player.cxx:          auto v = gameObjectPool.getVoxelGlobal({i, j, k});
./Player.cxx:          if (v && v->blockType != AIR)
./Player.cxx:            return true;
./Player.cxx:        }
./Player.cxx:    return false;
./Player.cxx:  };
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  glm::vec3 base = selfTransform.position;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(dx, 0, 0)))
./Player.cxx:    dx = 0;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(0, dy, 0)))
./Player.cxx:    dy = 0;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (overlaps(base + glm::vec3(0, 0, dz)))
./Player.cxx:    dz = 0;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (playerState.onGround) [[likely]]
./Player.cxx:    playerState.inJump = false;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  if (event.getKeyPressed(GLFW_KEY_SPACE) && playerState.onGround) {
./Player.cxx:    deltaJZ = 1.f;
./Player.cxx:    playerState.inJump = true;
./Player.cxx:  }
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  camera->cameraPos.x += dx;
./Player.cxx:  camera->cameraPos.y += dy;
./Player.cxx:  camera->cameraPos.z += dz;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  camera->locked = playerState.inInventory;
./Player.cxx:
./Player.cxx:  camera->updateUBO(UBO, swapChainExtent, event);
./Player.cxx:}

./PerlinNoise.hpp:	namespace perlin_detail
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		////////////////////////////////////////////////
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		//
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		//	These functions are provided for consistency.
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		//	You may get different results from std::shuffle() with different standard library implementations.
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		//
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		SIVPERLIN_CONCEPT_URBG
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline std::uint64_t Random(const std::uint64_t max, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return (urbg() % (max + 1));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class RandomIt, class URBG>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline void Shuffle(RandomIt first, RandomIt last, URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			if (first == last)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				return;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			using difference_type = typename std::iterator_traits<RandomIt>::difference_type;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			for (RandomIt it = first + 1; it < last; ++it)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				const std::uint64_t n = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(it - first);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				std::iter_swap(it, first + static_cast<difference_type>(Random(n, std::forward<URBG>(urbg))));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		//
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		////////////////////////////////////////////////
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float Fade(const Float t) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return t * t * t * (t * (t * 6 - 15) + 10);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float Lerp(const Float a, const Float b, const Float t) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return (a + (b - a) * t);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float Grad(const std::uint8_t hash, const Float x, const Float y, const Float z) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			const std::uint8_t h = hash & 15;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			const Float u = h < 8 ? x : y;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			const Float v = h < 4 ? y : h == 12 || h == 14 ? x : z;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return ((h & 1) == 0 ? u : -u) + ((h & 2) == 0 ? v : -v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float Remap_01(const Float x) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return (x * Float(0.5) + Float(0.5));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float Clamp_11(const Float x) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return std::clamp(x, Float(-1.0), Float(1.0));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float RemapClamp_01(const Float x) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			if (x <= Float(-1.0))
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				return Float(0.0);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			else if (Float(1.0) <= x)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				return Float(1.0);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return (x * Float(0.5) + Float(0.5));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Noise, class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline auto Octave1D(const Noise& noise, Float x, const std::int32_t octaves, const Float persistence) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			using value_type = Float;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type result = 0;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type amplitude = 1;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			for (std::int32_t i = 0; i < octaves; ++i)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				result += (noise.noise1D(x) * amplitude);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				x *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				amplitude *= persistence;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return result;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Noise, class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline auto Octave2D(const Noise& noise, Float x, Float y, const std::int32_t octaves, const Float persistence) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			using value_type = Float;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type result = 0;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type amplitude = 1;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			for (std::int32_t i = 0; i < octaves; ++i)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				result += (noise.noise2D(x, y) * amplitude);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				x *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				y *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				amplitude *= persistence;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return result;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Noise, class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline auto Octave3D(const Noise& noise, Float x, Float y, Float z, const std::int32_t octaves, const Float persistence) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			using value_type = Float;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type result = 0;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type amplitude = 1;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			for (std::int32_t i = 0; i < octaves; ++i)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				result += (noise.noise3D(x, y, z) * amplitude);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				x *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				y *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				z *= 2;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				amplitude *= persistence;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return result;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		[[nodiscard]]
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		inline constexpr Float MaxAmplitude(const std::int32_t octaves, const Float persistence) noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			using value_type = Float;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type result = 0;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			value_type amplitude = 1;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			for (std::int32_t i = 0; i < octaves; ++i)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				result += amplitude;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:				amplitude *= persistence;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:			return result;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	}

./PerlinNoise.hpp:	}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	SIVPERLIN_CONCEPT_URBG_
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	inline void BasicPerlinNoise<Float>::reseed(URBG&& urbg)
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		std::iota(m_permutation.begin(), m_permutation.end(), uint8_t{ 0 });
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		perlin_detail::Shuffle(m_permutation.begin(), m_permutation.end(), std::forward<URBG>(urbg));
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	}

./PerlinNoise.hpp:	template <class Float>
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	inline typename BasicPerlinNoise<Float>::value_type BasicPerlinNoise<Float>::noise3D(const value_type x, const value_type y, const value_type z) const noexcept
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	{
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type _x = std::floor(x);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type _y = std::floor(y);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type _z = std::floor(z);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::int32_t ix = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_x) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::int32_t iy = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_y) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::int32_t iz = static_cast<std::int32_t>(_z) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type fx = (x - _x);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type fy = (y - _y);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type fz = (z - _z);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type u = perlin_detail::Fade(fx);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type v = perlin_detail::Fade(fy);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type w = perlin_detail::Fade(fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t A = (m_permutation[ix & 255] + iy) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t B = (m_permutation[(ix + 1) & 255] + iy) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t AA = (m_permutation[A] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t AB = (m_permutation[(A + 1) & 255] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t BA = (m_permutation[B] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const std::uint8_t BB = (m_permutation[(B + 1) & 255] + iz) & 255;
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p0 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[AA], fx, fy, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p1 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[BA], fx - 1, fy, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p2 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[AB], fx, fy - 1, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p3 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[BB], fx - 1, fy - 1, fz);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p4 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(AA + 1) & 255], fx, fy, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p5 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(BA + 1) & 255], fx - 1, fy, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p6 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(AB + 1) & 255], fx, fy - 1, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type p7 = perlin_detail::Grad(m_permutation[(BB + 1) & 255], fx - 1, fy - 1, fz - 1);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type q0 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p0, p1, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type q1 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p2, p3, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type q2 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p4, p5, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type q3 = perlin_detail::Lerp(p6, p7, u);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type r0 = perlin_detail::Lerp(q0, q1, v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		const value_type r1 = perlin_detail::Lerp(q2, q3, v);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:
./PerlinNoise.hpp:		return perlin_detail::Lerp(r0, r1, w);
./PerlinNoise.hpp:	}
./PerlinNoise.hpp:

./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:VkVertexInputBindingDescription Vertex::getBindingDescription()
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:{
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    VkVertexInputBindingDescription bindingDescription{};
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // A vertex binding describes at which rate to load data from memory throughout the verticies.
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    // It specifies the number of bytes between data entries and whether to move to the next data entery after each vertex or after each instance.
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.binding = 0; // binding index to zero
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.stride = sizeof(Vertex);
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    bindingDescription.inputRate = VK_VERTEX_INPUT_RATE_VERTEX; // advance to the next input per vertex
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:    return bindingDescription;
./GraphicsPipeline.cxx:}

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::drawFrame()
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:{
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 1️⃣ Wait for previous frame to finish
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkWaitForFences(device, 1, &inFlightFences[currentFrame], VK_TRUE, UINT64_MAX);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkResetFences(device, 1, &inFlightFences[currentFrame]);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 2️⃣ Acquire an image from the swapchain
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    uint32_t imageIndex;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkResult res = vkAcquireNextImageKHR(
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        device,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        swapChain,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        UINT64_MAX,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        imageAvailableSemaphores[currentFrame], // still per-frame
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        VK_NULL_HANDLE,
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        &imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if (res != VK_SUCCESS && res != VK_SUBOPTIMAL_KHR)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    {
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to acquire swap chain image!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    }
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkResetCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], 0); // or VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_RESET_RELEASE_RESOURCES_BIT
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if(terrain->ready)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        updateUniformBuffer(currentFrame);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    recordCommandBuffer(commandBuffers[currentFrame], imageIndex);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 5️⃣ Submit the command buffer to the graphics queue
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSemaphore waitSemaphores[] = {imageAvailableSemaphores[currentFrame]};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkPipelineStageFlags waitStages[] = {VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_COLOR_ATTACHMENT_OUTPUT_BIT};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.waitSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pWaitSemaphores = waitSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pWaitDstStageMask = waitStages;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffers[currentFrame];
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // ✅ Use renderFinishedSemaphore per swapchain image
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSemaphore signalSemaphores[] = {renderFinishedSemaphores[imageIndex]};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.signalSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    submitInfo.pSignalSemaphores = signalSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if (vkQueueSubmit(graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, inFlightFences[currentFrame]) != VK_SUCCESS)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to submit draw command buffer!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 6️⃣ Present the image
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkPresentInfoKHR presentInfo{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PRESENT_INFO_KHR;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.waitSemaphoreCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pWaitSemaphores = signalSemaphores;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkSwapchainKHR swapChains[] = {swapChain};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.swapchainCount = 1;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pSwapchains = swapChains;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    presentInfo.pImageIndices = &imageIndex;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkQueuePresentKHR(presentQueue, &presentInfo);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // 7️⃣ Advance frame
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    currentFrame = (currentFrame + 1) % MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:}

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::recordCommandBuffer(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer, uint32_t imageIndex)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:{
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    {
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to begin recording command buffer!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    }
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    VkRenderPassBeginInfo renderPassInfo{};
