./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.renderPass = renderPass;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.framebuffer = swapChainFramebuffers[imageIndex];
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.renderArea.offset = {0, 0};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.renderArea.extent = swapChainExtent;
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    std::array<VkClearValue, 2> clearValues{};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    clearValues[0].color = {{0.102f, 0.133f, 0.255f, 1.0f}};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    clearValues[1].depthStencil = {1.0f, 0};
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.clearValueCount = static_cast<uint32_t>(clearValues.size());
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    renderPassInfo.pClearValues = clearValues.data();
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkCmdBeginRenderPass(commandBuffer, &renderPassInfo, VK_SUBPASS_CONTENTS_INLINE);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    DrawInfo drawInfoRay{commandBuffer, rayGraphicsPipeline.pipelineLayout, rayGraphicsPipeline.graphicsPipeline, descriptorSets, currentFrame, swapChainExtent};

./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkCmdBindPipeline(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, graphicsPipeline.graphicsPipeline);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    terrain->draw(commandBuffer, graphicsPipeline.pipelineLayout, graphicsPipeline.graphicsPipeline, descriptorSets, currentFrame, swapChainExtent);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // vkCmdBindPipeline(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, rayGraphicsPipeline.graphicsPipeline);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    // playerS1->camera->draw(drawInfoRay);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkCmdBindPipeline(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_BIND_POINT_GRAPHICS, uiRenderPipeline.graphicsPipeline);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    inventory->drawUI(drawInfoUI, playerS1->camera, ui.value());
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    playerS1->drawUIIfPossible(drawInfoUI, ui.value());
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    vkCmdEndRenderPass(commandBuffer);
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    if (vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer) != VK_SUCCESS)
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    {
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:        throw std::runtime_error("failed to record command buffer!");
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:    }
./HelloTriangleApplication.cxx:}

./Inventory.cxx:         (float(Inventory::dimensions.cw) / float(Inventory::dimensions.ww));

./Inventory.cxx:auto getHotbarCell = [](InventoryLayout &inventoryLayout,
./Inventory.cxx:                        glm::vec2 texture_start, glm::vec2 texture_end,
./Inventory.cxx:                        Event &event) {
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseX = event.mouseX;
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseY = event.mouseY;
./Inventory.cxx:  int px =
./Inventory.cxx:      int(mouseX - inventoryLayout.hotbar.leftMargin - texture_start.x) %
./Inventory.cxx:      int(inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth + inventoryLayout.hotbar.box_boxGap);
./Inventory.cxx:  bool hoveringBox =
./Inventory.cxx:      (px < inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth) &&
./Inventory.cxx:      (mouseY < (texture_end.y - inventoryLayout.hotbar.bottomMargin) &&
./Inventory.cxx:       (mouseY > (texture_end.y - inventoryLayout.hotbar.bottomMargin -
./Inventory.cxx:                  inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxHeight)));
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (mouseX >= texture_start.x && mouseX <= texture_end.x &&
./Inventory.cxx:      mouseY >= texture_start.y && mouseY <= texture_end.y) {
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:    if (hoveringBox) {
./Inventory.cxx:      int sx = mouseX - inventoryLayout.hotbar.leftMargin - texture_start.x;
./Inventory.cxx:      int cx = floor(int(sx / (inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth +
./Inventory.cxx:                               inventoryLayout.hotbar.box_boxGap)));
./Inventory.cxx:      return cx;
./Inventory.cxx:    }
./Inventory.cxx:  }
./Inventory.cxx:  return -1;
./Inventory.cxx:};
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:auto getInnerInventoryCell = [](InventoryLayout &inventoryLayout,
./Inventory.cxx:                                glm::vec2 texture_start, glm::vec2 texture_end,
./Inventory.cxx:                                Event &event) {
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseX = event.mouseX;
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseY = event.mouseY;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int numCols = inventoryLayout.hotbar.slots.size();
./Inventory.cxx:  int numRows = inventoryLayout.innerSlots.slots.size() / numCols;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int mx =
./Inventory.cxx:      int(mouseX - inventoryLayout.innerSlots.leftMargin - texture_start.x);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int px = mx % int(inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth +
./Inventory.cxx:                    inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.x);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int my =
./Inventory.cxx:      int(mouseY - texture_end.y + inventoryLayout.innerSlots.bottomMargin +
./Inventory.cxx:          (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight +
./Inventory.cxx:           inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y) *
./Inventory.cxx:              numRows -
./Inventory.cxx:          inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y);
./Inventory.cxx:  int py = my % int(inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight +
./Inventory.cxx:                    inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int row = std::floor(my / (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight +
./Inventory.cxx:                             inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y));
./Inventory.cxx:  int col = std::floor(mx / (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth +
./Inventory.cxx:                             inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.x));
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int idx = col + numCols * row;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (py >= inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight)
./Inventory.cxx:    return -1;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (px >= inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth)
./Inventory.cxx:    return -1;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (idx < 0)
./Inventory.cxx:    return -1;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (idx > inventoryLayout.innerSlots.slots.size() - 1)
./Inventory.cxx:    return -1;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  return idx;
./Inventory.cxx:};

./Inventory.cxx:Inventory::Inventory(VulkanContext &vkContext,
./Inventory.cxx:                     ApplicationDimensions &dimensions)
./Inventory.cxx:    : vkContext(vkContext), inventoryComponent(vkContext),
./Inventory.cxx:      filterComponent(vkContext) {
./Inventory.cxx:  // the image is 270*180
./Inventory.cxx:  Inventory::dimensions = dimensions;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.originalTextureWidth = 270;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.originalTextureHeight = 180;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  float aspect = float(dimensions.fbw) / float(dimensions.fbh);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  // the way orthographic projection is set up
./Inventory.cxx:  //  the canonical view port extends from - aspect to + aspect
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryComponent.setTextureIDX(0);
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryComponent.initUIComponent(
./Inventory.cxx:      glm::vec2(0), glm::vec2(dimensions.cw * scale, dimensions.ch * scale));
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  width_px = dimensions.ww * scale;
./Inventory.cxx:  height_px = dimensions.wh * scale;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x =
./Inventory.cxx:      width_px / inventoryLayout.originalTextureWidth;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y =
./Inventory.cxx:      height_px / inventoryLayout.originalTextureHeight;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  texture_start.x = abs(dimensions.ww - width_px) / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:  texture_end.x = abs(dimensions.ww + width_px) / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  texture_start.y = abs(dimensions.wh - height_px) / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:  texture_end.y = abs(dimensions.wh + height_px) / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("texture_start.x = {}", texture_start.x);
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("texture_end.x   = {}", texture_end.x);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("texture_start.y = {}", texture_start.y);
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("texture_end.y   = {}", texture_end.y);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("textureScaling: ({},{})", inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x,
./Inventory.cxx:               inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.hotbar.leftMargin = 4 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.hotbar.bottomMargin = 4 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.hotbar.box_boxGap = 2 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth = 20 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxHeight = 20 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.leftMargin = 4 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.bottomMargin =
./Inventory.cxx:      30 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap = glm::vec2(2.f);
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.x *= inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y *= inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth = 20 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.x;
./Inventory.cxx:  inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight = 20 * inventoryLayout.textureScaling.y;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  filterComponent.setTextureIDX(3);
./Inventory.cxx:  filterComponent.setEpsilonFactor_dz(1);
./Inventory.cxx:  filterComponent.initUIComponent(
./Inventory.cxx:      glm::vec2(0), glm::vec2(inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth * 1_px_to_u,
./Inventory.cxx:                              inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxHeight * 1_px_to_u));
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  // hotbar
./Inventory.cxx:  for (auto [i, slot] : std::views::enumerate(inventoryLayout.hotbar.slots)) {
./Inventory.cxx:    slot.bb.min.x = texture_start.x + inventoryLayout.hotbar.leftMargin +
./Inventory.cxx:                    i * (inventoryLayout.hotbar.box_boxGap +
./Inventory.cxx:                         inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth);
./Inventory.cxx:    slot.bb.max.x = slot.bb.min.x + inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxWidth;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:    slot.bb.min.y = texture_end.y - inventoryLayout.hotbar.bottomMargin -
./Inventory.cxx:                    inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxHeight;
./Inventory.cxx:    slot.bb.max.y = slot.bb.min.y + inventoryLayout.hotbar.boxHeight;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:    fmt::println("X : ({},{}) | Y : ({},{})", slot.bb.min.x, slot.bb.max.x,
./Inventory.cxx:                 slot.bb.min.y, slot.bb.max.y);
./Inventory.cxx:  }
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int numCols = inventoryLayout.hotbar.slots.size();
./Inventory.cxx:  int numRows = inventoryLayout.innerSlots.slots.size() / numCols;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  for (int o = 0; o < numRows; o++) {
./Inventory.cxx:    for (int i = 0; i < numCols; i++) {
./Inventory.cxx:      int idx = i + numCols * o;
./Inventory.cxx:      Slot &slot = inventoryLayout.innerSlots.slots[idx];
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:      slot.bb.min.x = texture_start.x + inventoryLayout.innerSlots.leftMargin +
./Inventory.cxx:                      i * (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.x +
./Inventory.cxx:                           inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth);
./Inventory.cxx:      slot.bb.max.x = slot.bb.min.x + inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxWidth;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:      slot.bb.min.y = texture_end.y - inventoryLayout.innerSlots.bottomMargin -
./Inventory.cxx:                      (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight +
./Inventory.cxx:                       inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y) *
./Inventory.cxx:                          numRows +
./Inventory.cxx:                      (inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight) * o +
./Inventory.cxx:                      inventoryLayout.innerSlots.box_boxGap.y * (o + 1);
./Inventory.cxx:      slot.bb.max.y = slot.bb.min.y + inventoryLayout.innerSlots.boxHeight;
./Inventory.cxx:    }
./Inventory.cxx:  }
./Inventory.cxx:}

./Inventory.cxx:void Inventory::inventoryUpdates(Event &event) {
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseX = event.mouseX;
./Inventory.cxx:  float mouseY = event.mouseY;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.x = dimensions.cw;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.y = dimensions.ch;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("voff_x: {}", voffset.x);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  int hotbarCell =
./Inventory.cxx:      getHotbarCell(inventoryLayout, texture_start, texture_end, event);
./Inventory.cxx:  int innverInventoryCell =
./Inventory.cxx:      getInnerInventoryCell(inventoryLayout, texture_start, texture_end, event);
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  if (hotbarCell < 0 && innverInventoryCell < 0)
./Inventory.cxx:    return;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  BoundingBox bb =
./Inventory.cxx:      hotbarCell < 0 ? inventoryLayout.innerSlots.slots[innverInventoryCell].bb
./Inventory.cxx:                     : inventoryLayout.hotbar.slots[hotbarCell].bb;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset = bb.max + bb.min;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset /= 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.x -= dimensions.fbw / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.y -= dimensions.fbh / 2.f;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.x /= dimensions.fbw;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.y /= dimensions.fbh;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.x *= dimensions.cw;
./Inventory.cxx:  voffset.y *= dimensions.ch;
./Inventory.cxx:
./Inventory.cxx:  fmt::println("vx: {} ", voffset.x);
./Inventory.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::createBuffer(VkDeviceSize size, VkBufferUsageFlags usage,
./Textures.cxx:                             VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties, VkBuffer &buffer,

./Textures.cxx:  VkBufferCreateInfo bufferInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_BUFFER_CREATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.size = size;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.usage = usage;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.sharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (vkCreateBuffer(device, &bufferInfo, nullptr, &buffer) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to create buffer!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:

./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_MEMORY_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.allocationSize = memRequirements.size;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.memoryTypeIndex =
./Textures.cxx:      findMemoryType(memRequirements.memoryTypeBits, properties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (vkAllocateMemory(device, &allocInfo, nullptr, &bufferMemory) !=
./Textures.cxx:      VK_SUCCESS) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate buffer memory!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkBindBufferMemory(device, buffer, bufferMemory, 0);
./Textures.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::createBuffer(VulkanContext vkContext, VkDeviceSize size,
./Textures.cxx:                             VkBufferUsageFlags usage,
./Textures.cxx:                             VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties, VkBuffer &buffer,
./Textures.cxx:                             VkDeviceMemory &bufferMemory) {
./Textures.cxx:  VkBufferCreateInfo bufferInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_BUFFER_CREATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.size = size;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.usage = usage;
./Textures.cxx:  bufferInfo.sharingMode = VK_SHARING_MODE_EXCLUSIVE;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (vkCreateBuffer(vkContext.device, &bufferInfo, nullptr, &buffer) !=
./Textures.cxx:      VK_SUCCESS) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to create buffer!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkMemoryRequirements memRequirements;
./Textures.cxx:  vkGetBufferMemoryRequirements(vkContext.device, buffer, &memRequirements);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkMemoryAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_MEMORY_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.allocationSize = memRequirements.size;
./Textures.cxx:  uint32_t typeFilter = memRequirements.memoryTypeBits;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./Textures.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(vkContext.physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++) {
./Textures.cxx:    if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags &
./Textures.cxx:                                    properties) == properties) {
./Textures.cxx:      allocInfo.memoryTypeIndex = i;
./Textures.cxx:      goto _ok;
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./Textures.cxx:_ok:;
./Textures.cxx:  if (vkAllocateMemory(vkContext.device, &allocInfo, nullptr, &bufferMemory) !=
./Textures.cxx:      VK_SUCCESS) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("failed to allocate buffer memory!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkBindBufferMemory(vkContext.device, buffer, bufferMemory, 0);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:uint32_t u_Texture::findMemoryType(uint32_t typeFilter,
./Textures.cxx:                                   VkMemoryPropertyFlags properties) {
./Textures.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties memProperties;
./Textures.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceMemoryProperties(physicalDevice, &memProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < memProperties.memoryTypeCount; i++) {
./Textures.cxx:    if ((typeFilter & (1 << i)) && (memProperties.memoryTypes[i].propertyFlags &
./Textures.cxx:                                    properties) == properties) {
./Textures.cxx:      return i;
./Textures.cxx:    }
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  throw std::runtime_error("failed to find suitable memory type!");
./Textures.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:      findMemoryType(memRequirements.memoryTypeBits, properties);

./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::createTextureImage() {
./Textures.cxx:  int texWidth, texHeight, texChannels;
./Textures.cxx:  stbi_uc *pixels = stbi_load(texturePath.c_str(), &texWidth, &texHeight,
./Textures.cxx:                              &texChannels, STBI_rgb_alpha);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  mipLevels = static_cast<uint32_t>(
./Textures.cxx:                  std::floor(std::log2(std::max(texWidth, texHeight)))) +
./Textures.cxx:              1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkDeviceSize imageSize = texWidth * texHeight * 4; // 4 -> r,g,b,a
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (!pixels) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("Failed to load image");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkBuffer stagingBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:  VkDeviceMemory stagingBufferMemory;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  createBuffer(imageSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:               VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT |
./Textures.cxx:                   VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_COHERENT_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:               stagingBuffer, stagingBufferMemory);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  void *data;
./Textures.cxx:  vkMapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, 0, imageSize, 0, &data);
./Textures.cxx:  memcpy(data, pixels, static_cast<size_t>(imageSize));
./Textures.cxx:  vkUnmapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  stbi_image_free(pixels);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  createImage(texWidth, texHeight, VK_SAMPLE_COUNT_1_BIT, mipLevels,
./Textures.cxx:              VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB, VK_IMAGE_TILING_OPTIMAL,
./Textures.cxx:              VK_IMAGE_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT |
./Textures.cxx:                  VK_IMAGE_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_IMAGE_USAGE_SAMPLED_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:              VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, textureImage,
./Textures.cxx:              textureImageMemory);
./Textures.cxx:  transitionImageLayout(textureImage, VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB,
./Textures.cxx:                        VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED,
./Textures.cxx:                        VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL, mipLevels);
./Textures.cxx:  copyBufferToImage(stagingBuffer, textureImage,
./Textures.cxx:                    static_cast<uint32_t>(texWidth),
./Textures.cxx:                    static_cast<uint32_t>(texHeight));
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  generateMipmaps(textureImage, VK_FORMAT_R8G8B8A8_SRGB, texWidth, texHeight,
./Textures.cxx:                  mipLevels);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkDestroyBuffer(device, stagingBuffer, nullptr);
./Textures.cxx:  vkFreeMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, nullptr);
./Textures.cxx:}

./Textures.cxx:VkCommandBuffer u_Texture::beginSingleTimeCommands() {
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBufferAllocateInfo allocInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_ALLOCATE_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.level = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_LEVEL_PRIMARY;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.commandPool = commandPool;
./Textures.cxx:  allocInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:  vkAllocateCommandBuffers(device, &allocInfo, &commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBufferBeginInfo beginInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  beginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_COMMAND_BUFFER_BEGIN_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  beginInfo.flags = VK_COMMAND_BUFFER_USAGE_ONE_TIME_SUBMIT_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkBeginCommandBuffer(commandBuffer, &beginInfo);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  return commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::endSingleTimeCommands(VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer) {
./Textures.cxx:  vkEndCommandBuffer(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkSubmitInfo submitInfo{};
./Textures.cxx:  submitInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SUBMIT_INFO;
./Textures.cxx:  submitInfo.commandBufferCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:  submitInfo.pCommandBuffers = &commandBuffer;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkQueueSubmit(graphicsQueue, 1, &submitInfo, VK_NULL_HANDLE);
./Textures.cxx:  vkQueueWaitIdle(graphicsQueue);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkFreeCommandBuffers(device, commandPool, 1, &commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:// before copying the image to the buffer we need to set it into the right
./Textures.cxx:// layout
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::transitionImageLayout(VkImage image, VkFormat format,
./Textures.cxx:                                      VkImageLayout oldLayout,
./Textures.cxx:                                      VkImageLayout newLayout,
./Textures.cxx:                                      uint32_t mipLevels) {
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.oldLayout = oldLayout;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.newLayout = newLayout;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  // We are not transfering queue family ownership rn!!!
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = mipLevels;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.srcAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.dstAccessMask = 0; // todo
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkPipelineStageFlags sourceStage;
./Textures.cxx:  VkPipelineStageFlags destinationStage;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_UNDEFINED &&
./Textures.cxx:      newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL) {
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcAccessMask = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    sourceStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TOP_OF_PIPE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    destinationStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  } else if (oldLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL &&
./Textures.cxx:             newLayout == VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL) {
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    sourceStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    destinationStage = VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  } else {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::invalid_argument("unsupported layout transition!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer, sourceStage, destinationStage, 0, 0,
./Textures.cxx:                       nullptr, 0, nullptr, 1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::copyBufferToImage(VkBuffer buffer, VkImage image,
./Textures.cxx:                                  uint32_t width, uint32_t height) {
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkBufferImageCopy region{};
./Textures.cxx:  region.bufferOffset = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  region.bufferRowLength = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  region.bufferImageHeight = 0;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageSubresource.mipLevel = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageOffset = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:  region.imageExtent = {width, height, 1};
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkCmdCopyBufferToImage(commandBuffer, buffer, image,
./Textures.cxx:                         VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL, 1, &region);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);
./Textures.cxx:}
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:void u_Texture::generateMipmaps(VkImage image, VkFormat imageFormat,
./Textures.cxx:                                int32_t texWidth, int32_t texHeight,
./Textures.cxx:                                uint32_t mipLevels) {
./Textures.cxx:  // Check if image format supports linear blitting
./Textures.cxx:  VkFormatProperties formatProperties;
./Textures.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceFormatProperties(physicalDevice, imageFormat,
./Textures.cxx:                                      &formatProperties);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  if (!(formatProperties.optimalTilingFeatures &
./Textures.cxx:        VK_FORMAT_FEATURE_SAMPLED_IMAGE_FILTER_LINEAR_BIT)) {
./Textures.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error(
./Textures.cxx:        "texture image format does not support linear blitting!");
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer commandBuffer = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.image = image;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  int32_t mipWidth = texWidth;
./Textures.cxx:  int32_t mipHeight = texHeight;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  for (uint32_t i = 1; i < mipLevels; i++) {
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:                         VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT, 0, 0, nullptr, 0,
./Textures.cxx:                         nullptr, 1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    VkImageBlit blit{};
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcOffsets[1] = {mipWidth, mipHeight, 1};
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcSubresource.mipLevel = i - 1;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.srcSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstOffsets[0] = {0, 0, 0};
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstOffsets[1] = {mipWidth > 1 ? mipWidth / 2 : 1,
./Textures.cxx:                          mipHeight > 1 ? mipHeight / 2 : 1, 1};
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstSubresource.mipLevel = i;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstSubresource.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./Textures.cxx:    blit.dstSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkCmdBlitImage(commandBuffer, image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL,
./Textures.cxx:                   image, VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL, 1, &blit,
./Textures.cxx:                   VK_FILTER_LINEAR);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_SRC_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:    barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:                         VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT, 0, 0, nullptr,
./Textures.cxx:                         0, nullptr, 1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:    if (mipWidth > 1)
./Textures.cxx:      mipWidth /= 2;
./Textures.cxx:    if (mipHeight > 1)
./Textures.cxx:      mipHeight /= 2;
./Textures.cxx:  }
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = mipLevels - 1;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:  barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  vkCmdPipelineBarrier(commandBuffer, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT,
./Textures.cxx:                       VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT, 0, 0, nullptr, 0,
./Textures.cxx:                       nullptr, 1, &barrier);
./Textures.cxx:
./Textures.cxx:  endSingleTimeCommands(commandBuffer);

./intiVk.cxx:static void printStackTrace() {
./intiVk.cxx:  static const int MAX_FRAMES = 20;
./intiVk.cxx:  void *frames[MAX_FRAMES];
./intiVk.cxx:  int frameCount = backtrace(frames, MAX_FRAMES);
./intiVk.cxx:  char **symbols = backtrace_symbols(frames, frameCount);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cerr << "  --- Stack Trace ---\n";
./intiVk.cxx:  for (int i = 1; i < frameCount; ++i) // skip frame 0 (this function itself)
./intiVk.cxx:  {
./intiVk.cxx:    std::string sym = symbols[i];
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    // Try to extract and demangle the mangled name
./intiVk.cxx:    // backtrace_symbols format: "./binary(_ZmangledName+0xoffset) [0xaddr]"
./intiVk.cxx:    size_t start = sym.find('(');
./intiVk.cxx:    size_t end = sym.find('+', start);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (start != std::string::npos && end != std::string::npos) {
./intiVk.cxx:      std::string mangled = sym.substr(start + 1, end - start - 1);
./intiVk.cxx:      int status = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:      char *demangled =
./intiVk.cxx:          abi::__cxa_demangle(mangled.c_str(), nullptr, nullptr, &status);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:      if (status == 0 && demangled) {
./intiVk.cxx:        std::cerr << "  #" << i << "  " << demangled << "  ("
./intiVk.cxx:                  << sym.substr(sym.find('[')) << "\n";
./intiVk.cxx:        free(demangled);
./intiVk.cxx:      } else {
./intiVk.cxx:        std::cerr << "  #" << i << "  " << sym << "\n";
./intiVk.cxx:      }
./intiVk.cxx:    } else {
./intiVk.cxx:      std::cerr << "  #" << i << "  " << sym << "\n";
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cerr << "  -------------------\n";
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  free(symbols);
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// finding if VL_LAYERS_KHRONOS_validation is there or not
./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::checkValidationLayerSupport() {
./intiVk.cxx:  uint32_t layerCount;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkEnumerateInstanceLayerProperties(&layerCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::vector<VkLayerProperties> availableLayers(layerCount);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkEnumerateInstanceLayerProperties(&layerCount, availableLayers.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  for (const char *layerName : validationLayers) {
./intiVk.cxx:    bool layerFound = false;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    for (auto &layerPorperties : availableLayers) {
./intiVk.cxx:      if (strcmp(layerName, layerPorperties.layerName) == 0) {
./intiVk.cxx:        layerFound = true;
./intiVk.cxx:        break;
./intiVk.cxx:      }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (!layerFound) {
./intiVk.cxx:      return false;
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return true;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:  for (const auto &device : devices) {

./intiVk.cxx:    candidates.insert(std::make_pair(score, device));
./intiVk.cxx:    std::cout << "Score: " << score << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  if (candidates.rbegin()->first > 0) {
./intiVk.cxx:    physicalDevice = candidates.rbegin()->second;
./intiVk.cxx:    msaaSamples = getMaxUsableSampleCount();
./intiVk.cxx:  } else {
./intiVk.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error("Failed to find a suitable GPU");
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// right now we only allow to use dedicated cards the support geometry shaders
./intiVk.cxx:// bool HelloTriangleApplication::isDeviceSuitable(VkPhysicalDevice device)
./intiVk.cxx:// {
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx://     // this controls which type of GPU to allow
./intiVk.cxx://     return deviceProperties.deviceType ==
./intiVk.cxx://     VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_DISCRETE_GPU && deviceFeatures.geometryShader;
./intiVk.cxx:// }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:int HelloTriangleApplication::rateDeviceSuitablity(VkPhysicalDevice device) {
./intiVk.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceProperties props;
./intiVk.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures feats;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceProperties(device, &props);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceFeatures(device, &feats);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  int score = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cout << "Device: " << props.deviceName << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Prefer discrete or integrated GPU
./intiVk.cxx:  if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_DISCRETE_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 20000;
./intiVk.cxx:  else if (props.deviceType == VK_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_TYPE_INTEGRATED_GPU)
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 5000;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Bigger textures = better
./intiVk.cxx:  score += props.limits.maxImageDimension2D;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Useful features
./intiVk.cxx:  if (feats.samplerAnisotropy)
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 1000;
./intiVk.cxx:  if (feats.shaderInt64)
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 500;
./intiVk.cxx:  if (feats.wideLines)
./intiVk.cxx:    score += 300;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:  // Metal backend doesn’t support geometry/tessellation shaders
./intiVk.cxx:  score += 1500;
./intiVk.cxx:#else
./intiVk.cxx:  if (!feats.geometryShader)
./intiVk.cxx:    return 0; // skip if no geometry shader
./intiVk.cxx:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return score;
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// Queue -> a line in which a set of commands needs to be executed
./intiVk.cxx:// there maybe multiple types of queues(Graphics, Computem, ...)
./intiVk.cxx:// Queue Family -> Conatains multiple queues for the GPU(Note: A queue family
./intiVk.cxx:// must be homogenous)
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// finding queue families
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::QueueFamilyIndices
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::findQueueFamilies(VkPhysicalDevice device) {
./intiVk.cxx:  QueueFamilyIndices indices;
./intiVk.cxx:  uint32_t queueFamilyCount = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(
./intiVk.cxx:      device, &queueFamilyCount,
./intiVk.cxx:      nullptr); // grts all the queue families supported by the GPU
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::vector<VkQueueFamilyProperties> queueFamilies(queueFamilyCount);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceQueueFamilyProperties(device, &queueFamilyCount,
./intiVk.cxx:                                           queueFamilies.data());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  int i = 0;
./intiVk.cxx:  for (const auto &queueFamily : queueFamilies) {
./intiVk.cxx:    if (queueFamily.queueFlags & VK_QUEUE_GRAPHICS_BIT)
./intiVk.cxx:      indices.graphicsFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkBool32 presentSupport = false;
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceSupportKHR(device, i, surface, &presentSupport);
./intiVk.cxx:    if (presentSupport)
./intiVk.cxx:      indices.presentFamily = i;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    if (indices.isComplete())
./intiVk.cxx:      break;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    i++;
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:  // NOTE: some GPU supports different graphics and presentation queues
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return indices;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:VkResult HelloTriangleApplication::CreateDebugUtilsMessengerEXT(
./intiVk.cxx:    VkInstance instance, const VkDebugUtilsMessengerCreateInfoEXT *pCreateInfo,
./intiVk.cxx:    const VkAllocationCallbacks *pAllocator,
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDebugUtilsMessengerEXT *pDebugMessenger) {
./intiVk.cxx:  auto func = (PFN_vkCreateDebugUtilsMessengerEXT)vkGetInstanceProcAddr(
./intiVk.cxx:      instance, "vkCreateDebugUtilsMessengerEXT");
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  if (func != nullptr)
./intiVk.cxx:    return func(instance, pCreateInfo, pAllocator, pDebugMessenger);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return VK_ERROR_EXTENSION_NOT_PRESENT;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::populateDebugMessengerCreateInfo(

./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.messageSeverity =
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_VERBOSE_BIT_EXT | // general diagnostics
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_WARNING_BIT_EXT | // likely bugs
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_ERROR_BIT_EXT;    // violations / crashes
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.messageType =
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_GENERAL_BIT_EXT |    // unrelated to spec
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_VALIDATION_BIT_EXT | // spec violations
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_PERFORMANCE_BIT_EXT; // non-optimal usage
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.pfnUserCallback = debugCallback;
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.pUserData = nullptr; // passed as pUserData in the callback
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
./intiVk.cxx:// The actual callback — Vulkan calls this whenever a message is generated.
./intiVk.cxx:// Returning VK_TRUE aborts the call that triggered the message (only useful
./intiVk.cxx:// for testing the validation layers themselves; keep it VK_FALSE normally).
./intiVk.cxx:// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
./intiVk.cxx:VKAPI_ATTR VkBool32 VKAPI_CALL HelloTriangleApplication::debugCallback(
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDebugUtilsMessageSeverityFlagBitsEXT messageSeverity,
./intiVk.cxx:    VkDebugUtilsMessageTypeFlagsEXT messageType,
./intiVk.cxx:    const VkDebugUtilsMessengerCallbackDataEXT *pCallbackData,
./intiVk.cxx:    void * /*pUserData*/) {
./intiVk.cxx:  const char *severity = "VERBOSE";
./intiVk.cxx:  if (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_ERROR_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    severity = "ERROR  ";
./intiVk.cxx:  else if (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_WARNING_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    severity = "WARNING";
./intiVk.cxx:  else if (messageSeverity & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_INFO_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    severity = "INFO   ";
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  const char *type = "GENERAL   ";
./intiVk.cxx:  if (messageType & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_VALIDATION_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    type = "VALIDATION";
./intiVk.cxx:  else if (messageType & VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_TYPE_PERFORMANCE_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    type = "PERF      ";
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cerr << "\n[VK " << severity << "][" << type << "] "
./intiVk.cxx:            << pCallbackData->pMessage << "\n";
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Print stack trace for warnings and errors only
./intiVk.cxx:  if (messageSeverity >= VK_DEBUG_UTILS_MESSAGE_SEVERITY_WARNING_BIT_EXT)
./intiVk.cxx:    printStackTrace();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return VK_FALSE;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createLogicalDevice() {

./intiVk.cxx:                                            indices.presentFamily.value()};

./intiVk.cxx:  for (uint32_t queueFamily : uniqueQueueFamilies) // prepare each queue family
./intiVk.cxx:  {

./intiVk.cxx:    queueCreateInfo.pQueuePriorities = &queuePriority;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    queueCreateInfos.push_back(
./intiVk.cxx:        queueCreateInfo); // push the queue info in the vector
./intiVk.cxx:  }

./intiVk.cxx:  // ---- Specifing which feature we wanna use ----

./intiVk.cxx:  vk12Features.descriptorIndexing = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:  vk12Features.shaderSampledImageArrayNonUniformIndexing = VK_TRUE;
./intiVk.cxx:  vk12Features.pNext = nullptr;
./intiVk.cxx:

./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_DEVICE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.queueCreateInfoCount =
./intiVk.cxx:      static_cast<uint32_t>(queueCreateInfos.size());
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.pQueueCreateInfos = queueCreateInfos.data();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  createInfo.pEnabledFeatures = &deviceFeatures;

./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::isDeviceSuitable(VkPhysicalDevice device) {
./intiVk.cxx:  QueueFamilyIndices indices = findQueueFamilies(device);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  bool extensionsSupported = checkDeviceExtensionSupport(device);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceDescriptorIndexingFeatures indexingSupport{};
./intiVk.cxx:  indexingSupport.sType =
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_DESCRIPTOR_INDEXING_FEATURES;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures2 features2{};
./intiVk.cxx:  features2.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_PHYSICAL_DEVICE_FEATURES_2;
./intiVk.cxx:  features2.pNext = &indexingSupport;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceFeatures2(physicalDevice, &features2);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  if (!indexingSupport.shaderSampledImageArrayNonUniformIndexing) {
./intiVk.cxx:    throw std::runtime_error(
./intiVk.cxx:        "Device does not support non-uniform texture indexing!");
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  bool swapChainAdequate = false;
./intiVk.cxx:  if (extensionsSupported) {
./intiVk.cxx:    SwapChainSupportDetails swapChainSupport = querySwapChainSupport(device);
./intiVk.cxx:    swapChainAdequate = !swapChainSupport.formats.empty() &&
./intiVk.cxx:                        !swapChainSupport.presentModes.empty();
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return indices.isComplete() && extensionsSupported && swapChainAdequate;
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:bool HelloTriangleApplication::checkDeviceExtensionSupport(
./intiVk.cxx:    VkPhysicalDevice device) {
./intiVk.cxx:  // ---- counting the number of extensions ----
./intiVk.cxx:  uint32_t extensionCount;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkEnumerateDeviceExtensionProperties(device, nullptr, &extensionCount,
./intiVk.cxx:                                       nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::vector<VkExtensionProperties> availableExtansions(extensionCount);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkEnumerateDeviceExtensionProperties(
./intiVk.cxx:      device, nullptr, &extensionCount,
./intiVk.cxx:      availableExtansions
./intiVk.cxx:          .data()); // all the required extensions are now retrived
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  std::set<std::string> requiredExtensions(deviceExtensions.begin(),
./intiVk.cxx:                                           deviceExtensions.end());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  for (const auto &extension : availableExtansions) {
./intiVk.cxx:    requiredExtensions.erase(extension.extensionName);
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // if all the required extensions are supported then the 'requiredExtension'
./intiVk.cxx:  // vector is empty which returns true
./intiVk.cxx:  return requiredExtensions.empty();
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// Swapchain -> A queue of images presented to the screen in a sequence
./intiVk.cxx:// Draw to an offscreen -> present it to the current window -> repeat
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// This function asks the GPU about the capablitie of the SwapChain that this
./intiVk.cxx:// GPU has
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::SwapChainSupportDetails
./intiVk.cxx:HelloTriangleApplication::querySwapChainSupport(VkPhysicalDevice device) {
./intiVk.cxx:  SwapChainSupportDetails details;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // ---- Get the capabilities ----
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceCapabilitiesKHR(device, surface,
./intiVk.cxx:                                            &details.capabilities);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // ---- get the format ----
./intiVk.cxx:  uint32_t formatCount;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceFormatsKHR(device, surface, &formatCount, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  if (formatCount != 0) {
./intiVk.cxx:    details.formats.resize(formatCount);
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfaceFormatsKHR(device, surface, &formatCount,
./intiVk.cxx:                                         details.formats.data());
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // ---- get the presentation mode(vsync, mailbox ...) ----
./intiVk.cxx:  uint32_t presentModeCount;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfacePresentModesKHR(device, surface, &presentModeCount,
./intiVk.cxx:                                            nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  if (presentModeCount != 0) {
./intiVk.cxx:    vkGetPhysicalDeviceSurfacePresentModesKHR(
./intiVk.cxx:        device, surface, &presentModeCount, details.presentModes.data());
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return details;
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// A swap suface define how pixels are stored(RGB vs BRGA or linear vs sRGB)
./intiVk.cxx:VkSurfaceFormatKHR HelloTriangleApplication::chooseSwapSurfaceFormat(
./intiVk.cxx:    const std::vector<VkSurfaceFormatKHR> &availableFormats) {
./intiVk.cxx:  {
./intiVk.cxx:    for (const auto &availableFormat : availableFormats) {
./intiVk.cxx:      if (availableFormat.format == VK_FORMAT_B8G8R8A8_SRGB &&
./intiVk.cxx:          availableFormat.colorSpace == VK_COLORSPACE_SRGB_NONLINEAR_KHR) {
./intiVk.cxx:        return availableFormat;
./intiVk.cxx:      }
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return availableFormats.at(0);
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:// Extent defines the resolution of the image
./intiVk.cxx:// MacOS has a fixed extent while other windowing systems have a varible extent
./intiVk.cxx:// which is clamped to the window bounds also High-DPI displays like Apple
./intiVk.cxx:// Liquid Retina displays have to be configure in a sepreate way
./intiVk.cxx:VkExtent2D HelloTriangleApplication::chooseSwapExtent(
./intiVk.cxx:    const VkSurfaceCapabilitiesKHR &capabilities) {
./intiVk.cxx:#ifdef __APPLE__
./intiVk.cxx:  // MoltenVK on macOS (Retina-safe)
./intiVk.cxx:  int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:  glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkExtent2D actualExtent = {static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:                             static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  return actualExtent; // Always use framebuffer size on Retina
./intiVk.cxx:#else
./intiVk.cxx:  // Metal IE: the size is predifined and is not UINT 32 max. therefore, use the
./intiVk.cxx:  // size provided by the system
./intiVk.cxx:  if (capabilities.currentExtent.width !=
./intiVk.cxx:      std::numeric_limits<uint32_t>::max()) {
./intiVk.cxx:    return capabilities.currentExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:  // The surface does not have a fixed size and you must create it by yourself
./intiVk.cxx:  else {
./intiVk.cxx:    int width, height;
./intiVk.cxx:    glfwGetFramebufferSize(_window, &width, &height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    VkExtent2D actualExtent = {static_cast<uint32_t>(width),
./intiVk.cxx:                               static_cast<uint32_t>(height)};
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    actualExtent.width =
./intiVk.cxx:        std::clamp(actualExtent.width, capabilities.minImageExtent.width,
./intiVk.cxx:                   capabilities.maxImageExtent.width);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    actualExtent.height =
./intiVk.cxx:        std::clamp(actualExtent.height, capabilities.minImageExtent.height,
./intiVk.cxx:                   capabilities.maxImageExtent.height);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:    return actualExtent;
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:#endif
./intiVk.cxx:}
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:// here we are using a staging buffer which is accisible by the CPU and then
./intiVk.cxx:// afterwards copying the contents of the staging buffer to the vertex buffer
./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createVertexBuffer() {
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cout << "Creating Vertex Buffer..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(vertices[0]) * vertices.size();
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkBuffer stagingBuffer;
./intiVk.cxx:  VkDeviceMemory stagingBufferMemory;
./intiVk.cxx:  // TX
./intiVk.cxx:  createBuffer(bufferSize, VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_SRC_BIT,
./intiVk.cxx:               VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_VISIBLE_BIT |
./intiVk.cxx:                   VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_HOST_CACHED_BIT,
./intiVk.cxx:               stagingBuffer, stagingBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // filling in the vertex buffer
./intiVk.cxx:  void *data;
./intiVk.cxx:  vkMapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, 0, bufferSize, 0, &data);
./intiVk.cxx:  memcpy(data, vertices.data(), (size_t)bufferSize);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkUnmapMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // creating the actul VBO and setting it up so the it is the destionation of
./intiVk.cxx:  // the transfer source TX
./intiVk.cxx:  createBuffer(
./intiVk.cxx:      bufferSize,
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_BUFFER_USAGE_TRANSFER_DST_BIT | VK_BUFFER_USAGE_VERTEX_BUFFER_BIT,
./intiVk.cxx:      VK_MEMORY_PROPERTY_DEVICE_LOCAL_BIT, vertexBuffer, vertexBufferMemory);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // but we still have to copy the memory contents manully
./intiVk.cxx:  copyBuffer(stagingBuffer, vertexBuffer, bufferSize);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  vkDestroyBuffer(device, stagingBuffer, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:  vkFreeMemory(device, stagingBufferMemory, nullptr);
./intiVk.cxx:}

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createUniformBuffers() {
./intiVk.cxx:  std::cout << "Creating Uniform Buffers..." << std::endl;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkDeviceSize bufferSize = sizeof(UniformBufferObject);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  uniformBuffers.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);

./intiVk.cxx:void HelloTriangleApplication::createSyncObject() {
./intiVk.cxx:  // 1️⃣ Per-frame semaphores for acquiring images
./intiVk.cxx:  imageAvailableSemaphores.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // 2️⃣ Per-swapchain-image semaphores for rendering completion
./intiVk.cxx:  renderFinishedSemaphores.resize(swapChainImages.size());
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // 3️⃣ Fences to limit frames in flight
./intiVk.cxx:  inFlightFences.resize(MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT);
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkSemaphoreCreateInfo semaphoreInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:  semaphoreInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_SEMAPHORE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  VkFenceCreateInfo fenceInfo{};
./intiVk.cxx:  fenceInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_FENCE_CREATE_INFO;
./intiVk.cxx:  fenceInfo.flags = VK_FENCE_CREATE_SIGNALED_BIT; // start signaled
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Create per-frame semaphores and fences
./intiVk.cxx:  for (size_t i = 0; i < MAX_FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT; i++) {
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkCreateSemaphore(device, &semaphoreInfo, nullptr,
./intiVk.cxx:                          &imageAvailableSemaphores[i]) != VK_SUCCESS ||
./intiVk.cxx:        vkCreateFence(device, &fenceInfo, nullptr, &inFlightFences[i]) !=
./intiVk.cxx:            VK_SUCCESS) {
./intiVk.cxx:      throw std::runtime_error("failed to create semaphore or fence!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:
./intiVk.cxx:  // Create per-swapchain-image render-finished semaphores
./intiVk.cxx:  for (size_t i = 0; i < swapChainImages.size(); i++) {
./intiVk.cxx:    if (vkCreateSemaphore(device, &semaphoreInfo, nullptr,
./intiVk.cxx:                          &renderFinishedSemaphores[i]) != VK_SUCCESS) {
./intiVk.cxx:      throw std::runtime_error("failed to create renderFinished semaphore!");
./intiVk.cxx:    }
./intiVk.cxx:  }
./intiVk.cxx:}

./2DTextureArray.cxx:void TextureArray2D::allocateStorageForTextures() {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  for (int i = 0; i < layerCount; i++) {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    int texWidth, texHeight, texChannels;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    stbi_uc *pixels = stbi_load(filePaths[i].c_str(), &texWidth, &texHeight,
./2DTextureArray.cxx:                                &texChannels, STBI_rgb_alpha);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    if (!pixels) {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:      throw std::runtime_error("Failed to load image");
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    }
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    // Allocate storage
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    blockTextures[i] = new unsigned char[textureWidth * textureHeight * 4];
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    // Copy into our array slot
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    memcpy(blockTextures[i], pixels, textureWidth * textureHeight * 4);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    stbi_image_free(pixels);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  }
./2DTextureArray.cxx:}
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:void TextureArray2D::uploadBlkTexturesToArray() {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const uint32_t TEX_COUNT = this->layerCount;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const uint32_t TEX_W = textureWidth;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const uint32_t TEX_H = textureHeight;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const uint32_t CHANNELS = 4;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const VkDeviceSize texSize = TEX_W * TEX_H * CHANNELS;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  const VkDeviceSize imageSize = texSize * TEX_COUNT;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  // 1. Map staging memory
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  void *data = nullptr;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  vkMapMemory(vkContext.device, stagingBlkBufferMemory, 0, imageSize, 0, &data);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  // 2. Copy all textures into one contiguous buffer
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < TEX_COUNT; i++) {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    memcpy(static_cast<char *>(data) + (i * texSize), blockTextures[i],
./2DTextureArray.cxx:           texSize);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  }
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  vkUnmapMemory(vkContext.device, stagingBlkBufferMemory);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  // 3. Record copy command
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer cmd = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  std::vector<VkBufferImageCopy> regions;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  regions.reserve(TEX_COUNT);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  for (uint32_t i = 0; i < TEX_COUNT; i++) {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    VkBufferImageCopy region{};
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.bufferOffset = i * texSize;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.mipLevel = 0;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.baseArrayLayer = i;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.imageSubresource.layerCount = 1;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    region.imageExtent = {TEX_W, TEX_H, 1};
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:    regions.push_back(region);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  }
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  vkCmdCopyBufferToImage(cmd, stagingBlkBuffer, blkTextureArrayImage,
./2DTextureArray.cxx:                         VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL,
./2DTextureArray.cxx:                         static_cast<uint32_t>(regions.size()), regions.data());
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  endSingleTimeCommands(cmd);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:}
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:void TextureArray2D::transitionBlkTextureArrayToShaderRead() {
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  VkCommandBuffer cmd = beginSingleTimeCommands();
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  VkImageMemoryBarrier barrier{};
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_IMAGE_MEMORY_BARRIER;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.oldLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_TRANSFER_DST_OPTIMAL;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.newLayout = VK_IMAGE_LAYOUT_SHADER_READ_ONLY_OPTIMAL;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.srcQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.dstQueueFamilyIndex = VK_QUEUE_FAMILY_IGNORED;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.image = blkTextureArrayImage;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.aspectMask = VK_IMAGE_ASPECT_COLOR_BIT;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseMipLevel = 0;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.levelCount = 1;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.baseArrayLayer = 0;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.subresourceRange.layerCount = this->layerCount;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  // IMPORTANT: synchronization masks
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.srcAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_TRANSFER_WRITE_BIT;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  barrier.dstAccessMask = VK_ACCESS_SHADER_READ_BIT;
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  vkCmdPipelineBarrier(cmd, VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_TRANSFER_BIT,
./2DTextureArray.cxx:                       VK_PIPELINE_STAGE_FRAGMENT_SHADER_BIT, 0, 0, nullptr, 0,
./2DTextureArray.cxx:                       nullptr, 1, &barrier);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:
./2DTextureArray.cxx:  endSingleTimeCommands(cmd);
./2DTextureArray.cxx:}
