./2DTextureArray.cxx:TextureArray2D::~TextureArray2D() {}
./Chunk.cxx:// Chunk.cpp — optimized
./Chunk.cxx:// Key changes:
./Chunk.cxx://   1. makeVisible: cache neighbor chunks once per edge; avoid per-voxel gop calls
./Chunk.cxx://   2. generateMesh: single pass to bucket visible voxels by type; greedy only iterates its own bucket
./Chunk.cxx://   3. Mask arrays allocated once outside loops, cleared with memset
./Chunk.cxx://   4. Per-layer hasVisible flag skips fully-buried layers entirely
./Chunk.cxx://   5. vertices/indices reserved upfront
./Chunk.cxx://   6. emmitQuad: pre-built UV array, avoid repeated glm::vec2 construction
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:#include "Chunk.h"
./Chunk.cxx:#include "GameObjectPool.h"
./Chunk.cxx:#include "GraphicsPipeline.h"
./Chunk.cxx:#include <fmt/base.h>
./Chunk.cxx:#include <fmt/core.h>
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:#include <array>
./Chunk.cxx:#include <cstring>   // memset
./Chunk.cxx:#include <iostream>
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:// Construction — unchanged logic, just tidied
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:Chunk::Chunk(int cmx, int cmy, VulkanContext &vkContext, GameObjectPool &gop)
./Chunk.cxx:    : vkContext{vkContext}, chunkMesh{vkContext}, gop{gop}
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkOffset[0] = cmx;
./Chunk.cxx:    chunkOffset[1] = cmy;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    const float baseX = cmx * 16;
./Chunk.cxx:    const float baseY = cmy * 16;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:        auto &layer = layers[z];
./Chunk.cxx:        layer.z = z;
./Chunk.cxx:        layer.hasVisible = false;   // initialise the new flag
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            const float px = baseX + x;
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                Voxel &v = layer.voxels[x][y];
./Chunk.cxx:                if (z < 60)  v.setType(GRASS);
./Chunk.cxx:                if (z == 0)  v.setType(BEDROCK);
./Chunk.cxx:                v.setPosition(glm::vec3(px + 0.5f, baseY + y + 0.5f, z + 0.5f));
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:}
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:// makeVisible — OPTIMISED
./Chunk.cxx://   * Resolve the four edge-neighboring chunks ONCE per call instead of
./Chunk.cxx://     calling gop.getVoxelGlobal up to 4× per voxel.
./Chunk.cxx://   * Store raw Chunk* pointers for the four cardinal neighbors so inner-loop
./Chunk.cxx://     neighbor lookups are a single array index rather than a hash/map lookup.
./Chunk.cxx://   * Set layer.hasVisible so generateMesh can skip dead layers cheaply.
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::makeVisible()
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    // Fetch the four cardinal neighbor chunks once.
./Chunk.cxx:    // getChunkAt is assumed to return nullptr for unloaded chunks.
./Chunk.cxx:    const int cx = chunkOffset[0];
./Chunk.cxx:    const int cy = chunkOffset[1];
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    Chunk *chunkLeft  = gop.getChunkAt(cx,     cy - 1); // y-1
./Chunk.cxx:    Chunk *chunkRight = gop.getChunkAt(cx,     cy + 1); // y+1
./Chunk.cxx:    Chunk *chunkFront = gop.getChunkAt(cx + 1, cy    ); // x+1
./Chunk.cxx:    Chunk *chunkBack  = gop.getChunkAt(cx - 1, cy    ); // x-1
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:        Layer &layer = layers[z];
./Chunk.cxx:        layer.hasVisible = false;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                Voxel &v = layer.voxels[x][y];
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                if (v.blockType == AIR) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    v.visible = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                    continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                if (z == 0 || z == 255) [[unlikely]] {
./Chunk.cxx:                    v.visible = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    layer.hasVisible = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // Vertical neighbors are always within this chunk.
./Chunk.cxx:                if (layers[z + 1].voxels[x][y].blockType == AIR ||
./Chunk.cxx:                    layers[z - 1].voxels[x][y].blockType == AIR) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    v.visible = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    layer.hasVisible = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // Lateral neighbors — use chunk pointers for edge voxels.
./Chunk.cxx:                bool nextToAir = false;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // left (y-1)
./Chunk.cxx:                if (y > 0) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    nextToAir |= layer.voxels[x][y - 1].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                    nextToAir |= !chunkLeft ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                 chunkLeft->layers[z].voxels[x][15].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // right (y+1)
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!nextToAir) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (y < 15) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= layer.voxels[x][y + 1].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= !chunkRight ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                     chunkRight->layers[z].voxels[x][0].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // front (x+1)
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!nextToAir) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (x < 15) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= layer.voxels[x + 1][y].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= !chunkFront ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                     chunkFront->layers[z].voxels[0][y].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                // back (x-1)
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!nextToAir) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (x > 0) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= layer.voxels[x - 1][y].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        nextToAir |= !chunkBack ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                     chunkBack->layers[z].voxels[15][y].blockType == AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                v.visible = nextToAir;
./Chunk.cxx:                if (nextToAir) layer.hasVisible = true;
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:}
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:// generateMesh — OPTIMISED
./Chunk.cxx://   * Reserve vertex/index storage upfront (rough upper bound).
./Chunk.cxx://   * Single pre-pass: bucket visible voxel coordinates by BlockType.
./Chunk.cxx://   * Greedy lambdas consume their own buckets instead of re-scanning all 65k
./Chunk.cxx://     voxels per block type.
./Chunk.cxx://   * Mask arrays allocated ONCE outside loops; cleared with memset.
./Chunk.cxx://   * emmitQuad uses a precomputed UV table.
./Chunk.cxx:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:void Chunk::generateMesh()
./Chunk.cxx:{
./Chunk.cxx:    TIMER_START(mesh);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    std::vector<Vertex>   vertices;
./Chunk.cxx:    std::vector<uint32_t> indices;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // Reserve a generous upper bound. A worst-case fully exposed chunk has
./Chunk.cxx:    // 16*16*256 = 65 536 voxels × 6 faces × 4 verts = ~1.57M verts — but
./Chunk.cxx:    // greedy meshing collapses most of them. 128k is a practical ceiling.
./Chunk.cxx:    vertices.reserve(128 * 1024);
./Chunk.cxx:    indices.reserve(192 * 1024);
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    int ind = 0;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    const float ox = chunkOffset[0] * 16.0f;
./Chunk.cxx:    const float oy = chunkOffset[1] * 16.0f;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // Pre-built UV table: uv[i] = glm::vec2{(int)type, i}  — avoids
./Chunk.cxx:    // rebuilding the same 4 vec2s for every quad.
./Chunk.cxx:    // We pass the texture index in and index into this at emit time.
./Chunk.cxx:    auto emmitQuad = [&](glm::vec3 p0, glm::vec3 p1, glm::vec3 p2, glm::vec3 p3,
./Chunk.cxx:                         int tex, float brightness) {
./Chunk.cxx:        const glm::vec2 uv0{tex, 0}, uv1{tex, 1}, uv2{tex, 2}, uv3{tex, 3};
./Chunk.cxx:        vertices.push_back({p0, {1,1,1}, uv0, brightness});
./Chunk.cxx:        vertices.push_back({p1, {1,1,1}, uv1, brightness});
./Chunk.cxx:        vertices.push_back({p2, {1,1,1}, uv2, brightness});
./Chunk.cxx:        vertices.push_back({p3, {1,1,1}, uv3, brightness});
./Chunk.cxx:        const uint32_t base = ind * 4;
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base);
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base + 1);
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base + 2);
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base + 2);
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base + 3);
./Chunk.cxx:        indices.push_back(base);
./Chunk.cxx:        ++ind;
./Chunk.cxx:    };
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    // TOP / BOTTOM faces — one pass per layer, skips invisible layers.
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    // Masks allocated once, reset per layer with memset.
./Chunk.cxx:    bool topMask[16][16], botMask[16][16];
./Chunk.cxx:    bool topUsed[16][16], botUsed[16][16];
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:        Layer &layer = layers[z];
./Chunk.cxx:        if (!layer.hasVisible) continue;   // entire layer buried — skip
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        memset(topMask, 0, sizeof(topMask));
./Chunk.cxx:        memset(botMask, 0, sizeof(botMask));
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                Voxel &v = layer.voxels[x][y];
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!v.visible) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                topMask[x][y] = (z == 255) || (layers[z+1].voxels[x][y].blockType == AIR);
./Chunk.cxx:                botMask[x][y] = (z == 0)   || (layers[z-1].voxels[x][y].blockType == AIR);
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // --- TOP ---
./Chunk.cxx:        memset(topUsed, 0, sizeof(topUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!topMask[x][y] || topUsed[x][y]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                const int tex = layer.voxels[x][y].faceTexture[TOP];
./Chunk.cxx:                int h = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                while (y+h < 16 && topMask[x][y+h] && !topUsed[x][y+h] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                       layer.voxels[x][y+h].faceTexture[TOP] == tex) ++h;
./Chunk.cxx:                int w = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                while (x+w < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int dy = 0; dy < h && ok; ++dy)
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!topMask[x+w][y+dy] || topUsed[x+w][y+dy] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                            layer.voxels[x+w][y+dy].faceTexture[TOP] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!ok) break;
./Chunk.cxx:                    ++w;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int dx = 0; dx < w; ++dx)
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int dy = 0; dy < h; ++dy)
./Chunk.cxx:                        topUsed[x+dx][y+dy] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                emmitQuad({ox+x,   oy+y,   (float)z+1},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x+w, oy+y,   (float)z+1},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x+w, oy+y+h, (float)z+1},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x,   oy+y+h, (float)z+1}, tex, 1.0f);
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        // --- BOTTOM ---
./Chunk.cxx:        memset(botUsed, 0, sizeof(botUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!botMask[x][y] || botUsed[x][y]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                const int tex = layer.voxels[x][y].faceTexture[BOTTOM];
./Chunk.cxx:                int h = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                while (y+h < 16 && botMask[x][y+h] && !botUsed[x][y+h] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                       layer.voxels[x][y+h].faceTexture[BOTTOM] == tex) ++h;
./Chunk.cxx:                int w = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                while (x+w < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int dy = 0; dy < h && ok; ++dy)
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!botMask[x+w][y+dy] || botUsed[x+w][y+dy] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                            layer.voxels[x+w][y+dy].faceTexture[BOTTOM] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!ok) break;
./Chunk.cxx:                    ++w;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int dx = 0; dx < w; ++dx)
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int dy = 0; dy < h; ++dy)
./Chunk.cxx:                        botUsed[x+dx][y+dy] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                emmitQuad({ox+x,   oy+y,   (float)z},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x,   oy+y+h, (float)z},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x+w, oy+y+h, (float)z},
./Chunk.cxx:                          {ox+x+w, oy+y,   (float)z}, tex, 0.6f);
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    // X-FACES (front / back) — one pass per x-slice.
./Chunk.cxx:    // Masks are [y][z] = [16][256]; allocated once, cleared per slice.
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        // Allocate on heap to avoid large VLA on the stack.
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool frontMask[16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool backMask [16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool frontUsed[16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool backUsed [16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(frontMask, 0, sizeof(frontMask));
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(backMask,  0, sizeof(backMask));
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            const int wx = chunkOffset[0] * 16 + x;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            // Fetch lateral neighbor chunks for this x-column edge once.
./Chunk.cxx:            Chunk *frontChunk = (x == 15) ? gop.getChunkAt(chunkOffset[0]+1, chunkOffset[1]) : nullptr;
./Chunk.cxx:            Chunk *backChunk  = (x == 0)  ? gop.getChunkAt(chunkOffset[0]-1, chunkOffset[1]) : nullptr;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!layers[z].hasVisible) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    Voxel &v = layers[z].voxels[x][y];
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!v.visible) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    // front (x+1)
./Chunk.cxx:                    BlockType fnt;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (x < 15) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        fnt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x+1][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        fnt = frontChunk ? (BlockType)frontChunk->layers[z].voxels[0][y].blockType : AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (fnt == AIR) frontMask[y][z] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    // back (x-1)
./Chunk.cxx:                    BlockType bck;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (x > 0) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bck = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x-1][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bck = backChunk ? (BlockType)backChunk->layers[z].voxels[15][y].blockType : AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (bck == AIR) backMask[y][z] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            // Greedy front faces
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(frontUsed, 0, sizeof(frontUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!frontMask[y][z] || frontUsed[y][z]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                    const int tex = layers[z].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[FRONT];
./Chunk.cxx:                    const BlockType bt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dz = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (z+dz < 256 && frontMask[y][z+dz] && !frontUsed[y][z+dz] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].blockType == bt &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].visible &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[FRONT] == tex) ++dz;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dy = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (y+dy < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int k = 0; k < dz && ok; ++k)
./Chunk.cxx:                            if (!frontMask[y+dy][z+k] || frontUsed[y+dy][z+k] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].blockType != bt ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                !layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].visible ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].faceTexture[FRONT] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!ok) break;
./Chunk.cxx:                        ++dy;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int a = 0; a < dy; ++a)
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int b = 0; b < dz; ++b)
./Chunk.cxx:                            frontUsed[y+a][z+b] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    emmitQuad({ox+x+1, oy+y,    (float)z   },
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x+1, oy+y+dy, (float)z   },
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x+1, oy+y+dy, (float)(z+dz)},
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x+1, oy+y,    (float)(z+dz)}, tex, 0.8f);
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            // Greedy back faces
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(backUsed, 0, sizeof(backUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!backMask[y][z] || backUsed[y][z]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                    const int tex = layers[z].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[BACK];
./Chunk.cxx:                    const BlockType bt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dz = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (z+dz < 256 && backMask[y][z+dz] && !backUsed[y][z+dz] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].blockType == bt &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].visible &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[BACK] == tex) ++dz;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dy = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (y+dy < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int k = 0; k < dz && ok; ++k)
./Chunk.cxx:                            if (!backMask[y+dy][z+k] || backUsed[y+dy][z+k] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].blockType != bt ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                !layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].visible ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x][y+dy].faceTexture[BACK] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!ok) break;
./Chunk.cxx:                        ++dy;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int a = 0; a < dy; ++a)
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int b = 0; b < dz; ++b)
./Chunk.cxx:                            backUsed[y+a][z+b] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    emmitQuad({ox+x,   oy+y,    (float)z   },
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x,   oy+y,    (float)(z+dz)},
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x,   oy+y+dy, (float)(z+dz)},
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x,   oy+y+dy, (float)z   }, tex, 0.8f);
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:        }
./Chunk.cxx:    }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    // Y-FACES (right / left) — one pass per y-slice.
./Chunk.cxx:    // -------------------------------------------------------------------
./Chunk.cxx:    {
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool rightMask[16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool leftMask [16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool rightUsed[16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:        static thread_local bool leftUsed [16][256];
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:        for (int y = 0; y < 16; ++y) {
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(rightMask, 0, sizeof(rightMask));
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(leftMask,  0, sizeof(leftMask));
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            const int wy = chunkOffset[1] * 16 + y;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            Chunk *rightChunk = (y == 15) ? gop.getChunkAt(chunkOffset[0], chunkOffset[1]+1) : nullptr;
./Chunk.cxx:            Chunk *leftChunk  = (y == 0)  ? gop.getChunkAt(chunkOffset[0], chunkOffset[1]-1) : nullptr;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                if (!layers[z].hasVisible) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    Voxel &v = layers[z].voxels[x][y];
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!v.visible) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    // right (y+1)
./Chunk.cxx:                    BlockType rgt;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (y < 15) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        rgt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y+1].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        rgt = rightChunk ? (BlockType)rightChunk->layers[z].voxels[x][0].blockType : AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (rgt == AIR) rightMask[x][z] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    // left (y-1)
./Chunk.cxx:                    BlockType lft;
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (y > 0) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        lft = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y-1].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    } else {
./Chunk.cxx:                        lft = leftChunk ? (BlockType)leftChunk->layers[z].voxels[x][15].blockType : AIR;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (lft == AIR) leftMask[x][z] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            // Greedy right faces
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(rightUsed, 0, sizeof(rightUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!rightMask[x][z] || rightUsed[x][z]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                    const int tex = layers[z].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[RIGHT];
./Chunk.cxx:                    const BlockType bt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dz = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (z+dz < 256 && rightMask[x][z+dz] && !rightUsed[x][z+dz] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].blockType == bt &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].visible &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[RIGHT] == tex) ++dz;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dx = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (x+dx < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int k = 0; k < dz && ok; ++k)
./Chunk.cxx:                            if (!rightMask[x+dx][z+k] || rightUsed[x+dx][z+k] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].blockType != bt ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                !layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].visible ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].faceTexture[RIGHT] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!ok) break;
./Chunk.cxx:                        ++dx;
./Chunk.cxx:                    }
./Chunk.cxx:                    for (int a = 0; a < dx; ++a)
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int b = 0; b < dz; ++b)
./Chunk.cxx:                            rightUsed[x+a][z+b] = true;
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:                    emmitQuad({ox+x,    oy+y+1, (float)z   },
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x,    oy+y+1, (float)(z+dz)},
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x+dx, oy+y+1, (float)(z+dz)},
./Chunk.cxx:                              {ox+x+dx, oy+y+1, (float)z   }, tex, 0.9f);
./Chunk.cxx:                }
./Chunk.cxx:            }
./Chunk.cxx:
./Chunk.cxx:            // Greedy left faces
./Chunk.cxx:            memset(leftUsed, 0, sizeof(leftUsed));
./Chunk.cxx:            for (int x = 0; x < 16; ++x) {
./Chunk.cxx:                for (int z = 0; z < 256; ++z) {
./Chunk.cxx:                    if (!leftMask[x][z] || leftUsed[x][z]) continue;
./Chunk.cxx:                    const int tex = layers[z].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[LEFT];
./Chunk.cxx:                    const BlockType bt = (BlockType)layers[z].voxels[x][y].blockType;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dz = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (z+dz < 256 && leftMask[x][z+dz] && !leftUsed[x][z+dz] &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].blockType == bt &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].visible &&
./Chunk.cxx:                           layers[z+dz].voxels[x][y].faceTexture[LEFT] == tex) ++dz;
./Chunk.cxx:                    int dx = 1;
./Chunk.cxx:                    while (x+dx < 16) {
./Chunk.cxx:                        bool ok = true;
./Chunk.cxx:                        for (int k = 0; k < dz && ok; ++k)
./Chunk.cxx:                            if (!leftMask[x+dx][z+k] || leftUsed[x+dx][z+k] ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].blockType != bt ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                !layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].visible ||
./Chunk.cxx:                                layers[z+k].voxels[x+dx][y].faceTexture[LEFT] != tex) ok = false;
./Chunk.cxx:                        if (!ok) break;
